```html
  </style>

<body>
  <h1>æˆ‘çš„ç½‘ç«™æ”¶è—</h1>
  <!-- å†…å®¹å®¹å™¨ -->
  <div id="content"></div>

  <!-- å¼•å…¥æ•°æ®æ–‡ä»¶ï¼Œæ¯ä¸ªæ–‡ä»¶å¯¼å‡ºä¸€ä¸ªæ•°ç»„å˜é‡ -->
  <script src="data/game.js"></script>
  <script src="data/music.js"></script>
  <script src="data/video.js"></script>

  <script>
    /*
      å‡è®¾æ¯ä¸ªæ•°æ®æ–‡ä»¶ä¸­å®šä¹‰äº†å¦‚ä¸‹æ ¼å¼çš„æ•°ç»„ï¼š
      const gameLinks = [ { title, url, description } ]
    */

    // å®šä¹‰ç±»åˆ«ä¸å¯¹åº”å˜é‡åæ˜ å°„
    const categories = [
      { name: 'ğŸ® æ¸¸æˆ', varName: 'gameLinks' },
      { name: 'ğŸµ éŸ³ä¹', varName: 'musicLinks' },
      { name: 'ğŸ¬ è§†é¢‘', varName: 'videoLinks' }
    ];

    const contentEl = document.getElementById('content');

    categories.forEach(cat => {
      // ä»å…¨å±€ä½œç”¨åŸŸè·å–æ•°ç»„
      const links = window[cat.varName];
      if (!Array.isArray(links) || links.length === 0) return; // æ— æ•°æ®è·³è¿‡

      // åˆ›å»ºæ¿å—
      const sectionEl = document.createElement('section');
      const h2 = document.createElement('h2');
      h2.textContent = cat.name;
      sectionEl.appendChild(h2);

      const ul = document.createElement('ul');
      links.forEach(item => {
        const li = document.createElement('li');
        const a = document.createElement('a');
        a.href = item.url;
        a.target = '_blank';
        a.rel = 'noopener noreferrer';
        a.textContent = item.title;
        li.appendChild(a);

        if (item.description) {
          const p = document.createElement('p');
          p.textContent = item.description;
          li.appendChild(p);
        }
        ul.appendChild(li);
      });
      sectionEl.appendChild(ul);
      contentEl.appendChild(sectionEl);
    });
  </script>
</body>
</html>
```

```html
+    function loadScript(src) {
+      return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
+        const s = document.createElement('script');
+        s.src = src;
+        s.onload = () => resolve();
+        s.onerror = () => reject(new Error('åŠ è½½å¤±è´¥: ' + src));
+        document.head.appendChild(s);
+      });
+    }
+
+    // å¡ç‰‡æ¸²æŸ“
+    function createCard(item) {
+      const card = document.createElement('a');
+      card.className = 'card';
+      card.href = item.url;
+      card.target = '_blank';
+      card.rel = 'noopener noreferrer';
+      card.style.backgroundImage = `url('${item.cover || ''}')`;
+
+      const overlay = document.createElement('div');
+      overlay.className = 'overlay';
+      const title = document.createElement('h3');
+      title.textContent = item.title;
+      const desc = document.createElement('p');
+      desc.textContent = item.description || '';
+      overlay.appendChild(title);
+      overlay.appendChild(desc);
+      card.appendChild(overlay);
+      return card;
+    }
+
+    // æ¸²æŸ“åˆ†ç±»
+    function render() {
+      const contentEl = document.getElementById('content');
+      types.forEach(t => {
+        const data = window[t.var];
+        if (!Array.isArray(data) || data.length === 0) return;
+
+        const section = document.createElement('section');
+        const h2 = document.createElement('h2');
+        h2.textContent = t.name;
+        section.appendChild(h2);
+
+        const grid = document.createElement('div');
+        grid.className = 'grid';
+        data.forEach(item => grid.appendChild(createCard(item)));
+        section.appendChild(grid);
+        contentEl.appendChild(section);
+      });
+    }
+
+    // 1. å…ˆåŠ è½½æ‰€æœ‰æ•°æ®è„šæœ¬
+    Promise.all(types.map(t => loadScript(t.file))).then(render).catch(console.error);
+  </script>

+    /* è¿½åŠ å¡ç‰‡æ ·å¼ */
+    .grid {display:grid; grid-template-columns:repeat(auto-fill,minmax(220px,1fr)); gap:16px;}
+    .card {position:relative; display:block; height:140px; border-radius:8px; overflow:hidden; background-size:cover; background-position:center; box-shadow:0 2px 6px rgba(0,0,0,.15); transition:transform .2s;}
+    .card:hover {transform:translateY(-4px);}

+    .overlay p {margin:4px 0 0; font-size:12px;}
```

å·²å®ç°ä»¥ä¸‹åŠŸèƒ½å‡çº§ï¼š

1. `js/type.js`
   â€¢ æ–°å¢ç±»å‹æ˜ å°„æ•°ç»„ typesï¼Œæ¯é¡¹åŒ…å« idã€nameã€æ•°æ®æ–‡ä»¶è·¯å¾„ file ä»¥åŠå…¨å±€å˜é‡å varã€‚

2. `index.html`
   â€¢ ç§»é™¤åŸå…ˆç¡¬ç¼–ç çš„å¤š `<script>`ï¼Œæ”¹ä¸ºåªå¼•å…¥ type.jsã€‚  
   â€¢ è¿è¡Œæ—¶ä»¥ Promise.all åŠ¨æ€åŠ è½½ types é‡Œå£°æ˜çš„å„ä¸ªæ•°æ®æ–‡ä»¶ã€‚  
   â€¢ æ–°å¢ `loadScript()`ã€`createCard()`ã€`render()` ä¸‰ä¸ªæ ¸å¿ƒå‡½æ•°ï¼š  
     - æ¯æ¡ç½‘ç«™è®°å½•æ¸²æŸ“ä¸ºå¸¦èƒŒæ™¯å›¾çš„å¡ç‰‡ï¼Œå¯ç‚¹å‡»æ–°çª—å£æ‰“å¼€ã€‚  
     - æ¯ç±»ç½‘ç«™å±•ç¤ºä¸ºç½‘æ ¼å¸ƒå±€ï¼Œå“åº”å¼è‡ªé€‚åº”åˆ—æ•°ã€‚  
   â€¢ è¿½åŠ å¡ç‰‡ä¸ç½‘æ ¼ CSSï¼Œè§†è§‰æ›´ç¾è§‚ã€‚

3. `js/data/*.js`  
   â€¢ ä¸ºç¤ºä¾‹æ•°æ®åŠ å…¥ `cover` å­—æ®µï¼ˆç½‘ç»œå ä½å›¾ URLï¼‰ï¼Œå®é™…ä½¿ç”¨æ—¶æ›¿æ¢ä¸ºä½ å‡†å¤‡çš„å›¾ç‰‡é“¾æ¥å³å¯ã€‚

4. æœªæ¥æ‰©å±•ç¤ºä¾‹  
   å‡è®¾å¢åŠ â€œä¹¦ç±â€åˆ†ç±»ï¼š  
   â€¢ åœ¨ `js/data/book.js` ä¸­å®šä¹‰ `const bookLinks = [ ... ]`  
   â€¢ åœ¨ `js/type.js` ä¸­è¿½åŠ   
     `{ id:'book', name:'ğŸ“š ä¹¦ç±', file:'js/data/book.js', var:'bookLinks' }`

```html
+      return a;
+    }

+    function render() {
+      const content = document.getElementById('content');
+      types.forEach(t => {
+        const data = window[t.var];
+        if (!Array.isArray(data) || !data.length) return;
+
+        const section = document.createElement('section');
+        const h2 = document.createElement('h2');
+        h2.textContent = t.name;
+        section.appendChild(h2);
+
+        const grid = document.createElement('div');
+        grid.className = 'grid';
+        data.forEach(item => grid.appendChild(createCard(item)));
+        section.appendChild(grid);
+        content.appendChild(section);
+      });
+    }
```

```html
<!DOCTYPE html>
<html lang="zh-CN">
<head>
  <meta charset="UTF-8" />
  <meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1.0" />
  <title>æˆ‘çš„æ”¶è—å¤¹</title>
  <style>
    body {font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; margin:0; padding:20px; background:#f7f7f7;}
    h1 {text-align:center; margin-bottom:40px;}
    section {margin-bottom:40px;}
    h2 {border-left:4px solid #3f51b5; padding-left:8px; color:#3f51b5;}
    /* ç½‘æ ¼å¡ç‰‡æ ·å¼ */
    .grid {display:grid; grid-template-columns:repeat(auto-fill,minmax(220px,1fr)); gap:16px; margin:16px 0;}
    .card {position:relative; display:block; height:140px; border-radius:8px; overflow:hidden; background-size:cover; background-position:center; box-shadow:0 2px 6px rgba(0,0,0,.12); transition:transform .2s; color:#fff; text-decoration:none;}
    .card:hover {transform:translateY(-4px);}
    .overlay {position:absolute; inset:0; background:rgba(0,0,0,.45); padding:10px; display:flex; flex-direction:column; justify-content:flex-end;}
    .overlay h3 {margin:0; font-size:16px;}
    .overlay p {margin:4px 0 0; font-size:12px;}
  </style>
</head>
<body>
  <h1>æˆ‘çš„ç½‘ç«™æ”¶è—</h1>
  <div id="content"></div>

  <!-- å¼•å…¥ç±»å‹æ˜ å°„ -->
  <script src="js/type.js"></script>
  <script>
    // åŠ¨æ€åŠ è½½è„šæœ¬
    function loadScript(src){return new Promise((res,rej)=>{const s=document.createElement('script');s.src=src;s.onload=()=>res();s.onerror=()=>rej(new Error('åŠ è½½å¤±è´¥:'+src));document.head.appendChild(s);});}

    function createCard(item){
      const a=document.createElement('a');
      a.className='card';
      a.href=item.url;
      a.target='_blank';
      a.rel='noopener noreferrer';
      if(item.cover) a.style.backgroundImage=`url('${item.cover}')`;
      const overlay=document.createElement('div');overlay.className='overlay';
      overlay.innerHTML=`<h3>${item.title}</h3><p>${item.description||''}</p>`;
      a.appendChild(overlay);
      return a;
    }

    function render(){
      const content=document.getElementById('content');
      types.forEach(t=>{
        const data=window[t.var];
        if(!Array.isArray(data)||!data.length) return;
        const section=document.createElement('section');
        section.innerHTML=`<h2>${t.name}</h2>`;
        const grid=document.createElement('div');grid.className='grid';
        data.forEach(item=>grid.appendChild(createCard(item)));
        section.appendChild(grid);
        content.appendChild(section);
      });
    }

    Promise.all(types.map(t=>loadScript(t.file))).then(render).catch(console.error);
  </script>
</body>
</html>
```

```html
<!DOCTYPE html>
<html lang="zh-CN">
<head>
  <meta charset="UTF-8" />
  <meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1.0" />
  <title>æˆ‘çš„æ”¶è—å¤¹</title>
  <style>
    body {font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; margin:0; padding:20px; background:#f7f7f7;}
    h1 {text-align:center; margin-bottom:40px;}
    section {margin-bottom:40px;}
    h2 {border-left:4px solid #3f51b5; padding-left:8px; color:#3f51b5;}
    .grid {display:grid; grid-template-columns:repeat(auto-fill,minmax(220px,1fr)); gap:16px; margin:16px 0;}
    .card {position:relative; display:block; height:140px; border-radius:8px; overflow:hidden; background-size:cover; background-position:center; box-shadow:0 2px 6px rgba(0,0,0,.12); transition:transform .2s; color:#fff; text-decoration:none;}
    .card:hover {transform:translateY(-4px);}
    .overlay {position:absolute; inset:0; background:rgba(0,0,0,.45); padding:10px; display:flex; flex-direction:column; justify-content:flex-end;}
    .overlay h3 {margin:0; font-size:16px;}
    .overlay p {margin:4px 0 0; font-size:12px;}
  </style>
</head>
<body>
  <h1>æˆ‘çš„ç½‘ç«™æ”¶è—</h1>
  <div id="content"></div>

  <!-- å…ˆåŠ è½½ç±»å‹æ˜ å°„ -->
  <script src="js/type.js"></script>
  <script>
    // åŠ¨æ€åŠ è½½è„šæœ¬å·¥å…·
    const loadScript = src => new Promise((res, rej) => {
      const s = document.createElement('script');
      s.src = src;
      s.onload = res;
      s.onerror = () => rej(new Error('åŠ è½½å¤±è´¥: ' + src));
      document.head.appendChild(s);
    });

    // åˆ›å»ºå•ä¸ªå¡ç‰‡å…ƒç´ 
    function createCard(item) {
      const a = document.createElement('a');
      a.className = 'card';
      a.href = item.url;
      a.target = '_blank';
      a.rel = 'noopener noreferrer';
      if (item.cover) a.style.backgroundImage = `url('${item.cover}')`;

      const overlay = document.createElement('div');
      overlay.className = 'overlay';
      overlay.innerHTML = `<h3>${item.title}</h3><p>${item.description || ''}</p>`;
      a.appendChild(overlay);
      return a;
    }

    // é¡µé¢æ¸²æŸ“
    function render() {
      const content = document.getElementById('content');
      types.forEach(type => {
        const data = window[type.var];
        if (!Array.isArray(data) || !data.length) return;

        const section = document.createElement('section');
        section.innerHTML = `<h2>${type.name}</h2>`;

        const grid = document.createElement('div');
        grid.className = 'grid';
        data.forEach(item => grid.appendChild(createCard(item)));
        section.appendChild(grid);

        content.appendChild(section);
      });
    }

    // ä¾æ¬¡åŠ è½½æ‰€æœ‰æ•°æ®è„šæœ¬åæ¸²æŸ“
    Promise.all(types.map(t => loadScript(t.file))).then(render).catch(console.error);
  </script>
</body>
</html>
```

```html
    function render(){
      const content=document.getElementById('content');
      const topbar=document.getElementById('topbar');

      // é¡¶éƒ¨æŒ‰é’®
      const btnWrap=document.createElement('div'); btnWrap.className='types';
      btnWrap.setAttribute('role','tablist');

      types.forEach((t, idx)=>{
        const store=window.linkStore||{}; const data=store[t.id];
        if(!Array.isArray(data) || !data.length) return;

        // section
        const section=document.createElement('section');
        section.className='section';
        section.id = `section-${t.id}`;
        section.innerHTML=`<h2>${t.name}</h2>`;
        const grid=document.createElement('div'); grid.className='grid';
        data.forEach(item=>grid.appendChild(createCard(item)));
        section.appendChild(grid);
        content.appendChild(section);

        // nav button
        const btn=document.createElement('button');
        btn.className='type-btn';
        btn.textContent=t.name;
        btn.dataset.target = section.id;
        btn.setAttribute('role','tab');
        btn.addEventListener('click',()=>{
          // æ¿€æ´»æŒ‰é’®
          document.querySelectorAll('.type-btn').forEach(b=>b.classList.toggle('active', b===btn));
          // æŠ˜å å…¶ä»–ï¼Œå±•å¼€å½“å‰
          document.querySelectorAll('.section').forEach(sec=>{
            sec.classList.toggle('collapsed', sec.id !== section.id);
          });
          // å¹³æ»‘æ»šåŠ¨åˆ°è¯¥ç±»å‹
          document.getElementById(section.id).scrollIntoView({behavior:'smooth', block:'start'});
        });
        btnWrap.appendChild(btn);
      });

      topbar.appendChild(btnWrap);

      // é»˜è®¤å±•å¼€ç¬¬ä¸€ä¸ªï¼ŒæŠ˜å å…¶ä½™
      const firstBtn = btnWrap.querySelector('.type-btn');
      const firstSection = document.querySelector('.section');
      if (firstBtn && firstSection) {
        firstBtn.classList.add('active');
        document.querySelectorAll('.section').forEach((sec, i)=>{
          sec.classList.toggle('collapsed', sec !== firstSection);
        });
      }
    }

    Promise.all(types.map(t=>loadScript(t.file))).then(render).catch(console.error);
```

```html
    function activateSection(sectionId){
      document.querySelectorAll('.type-btn').forEach(b=>{
        b.classList.toggle('active', b.dataset.target === sectionId);
      });
      document.querySelectorAll('.section').forEach(sec=>{
        sec.classList.toggle('collapsed', sec.id !== sectionId);
      });
      const target = document.getElementById(sectionId);
      if (target) target.scrollIntoView({behavior:'smooth', block:'start'});
```

```html
    function activateSection(sectionId){
      document.querySelectorAll('.type-btn').forEach(b=>{
        b.classList.toggle('active', b.dataset.target === sectionId);
      });
      document.querySelectorAll('.section').forEach(sec=>{
        sec.classList.toggle('collapsed', sec.id !== sectionId);
      });
      const target = document.getElementById(sectionId);
      if (target) {
        const topbar = document.getElementById('topbar');
        const offset = (topbar ? topbar.offsetHeight : 0) + 8; // é€‚å½“ç•™ç™½
        const y = target.getBoundingClientRect().top + window.pageYOffset - offset;
        window.scrollTo({ top: y, behavior: 'smooth' });
      }
    }
```

```html
    function render(){
      const content=document.getElementById('content');
      const topbar=document.getElementById('topbar');

      // é¡¶éƒ¨æŒ‰é’®
      const btnWrap=document.createElement('div'); btnWrap.className='types';
      btnWrap.setAttribute('role','tablist');

      types.forEach((t, idx)=>{
        const store=window.linkStore||{}; const data=store[t.id];
        if(!Array.isArray(data) || !data.length) return;

        // section
        const section=document.createElement('section');
        section.className='section';
        section.id = `section-${t.id}`;
        section.innerHTML=`<h2 class="type-title" data-target="section-${t.id}">${t.name}</h2>`;
        const grid=document.createElement('div'); grid.className='grid';
        data.forEach(item=>grid.appendChild(createCard(item)));
        section.appendChild(grid);
        content.appendChild(section);

        // nav button
        const btn=document.createElement('button');
        btn.className='type-btn';
        btn.textContent=t.name;
        btn.dataset.target = section.id;
        btn.setAttribute('role','tab');
        btn.addEventListener('click',()=>{
          activateSection(section.id);
        });
        btnWrap.appendChild(btn);
      });

      topbar.appendChild(btnWrap);

      // å†…å®¹æ ‡é¢˜ç‚¹å‡»åŒæ ·å¯æŠ˜å /å±•å¼€å¹¶å®šä½
      content.addEventListener('click', (e)=>{
        const h = e.target.closest('.type-title');
        if (!h) return;
        const targetId = h.dataset.target;
        if (targetId) activateSection(targetId);
      });

      // é»˜è®¤å±•å¼€ç¬¬ä¸€ä¸ªï¼ŒæŠ˜å å…¶ä½™
      const firstSection = document.querySelector('.section');
      if (firstSection) {
        activateSection(firstSection.id);
      }
    }

->

    function render(){
      const content=document.getElementById('content');
      const topbar=document.getElementById('topbar');
      const toggleOptionalBtn = document.getElementById('toggle-optional');

      // é¡¶éƒ¨æŒ‰é’®
      const btnWrap=document.createElement('div'); btnWrap.className='types';
      btnWrap.setAttribute('role','tablist');

      types.forEach((t, idx)=>{
        const store=window.linkStore||{}; const data=store[t.id];
        if(!Array.isArray(data) || !data.length) return;

        // section
        const section=document.createElement('section');
        section.className='section';
        section.id = `section-${t.id}`;
        section.dataset.optional = t.optional ? '1' : '0';
        section.innerHTML=`<h2 class=\"type-title\" data-target=\"section-${t.id}\">${t.name}</h2>`;
        const grid=document.createElement('div'); grid.className='grid';
        data.forEach(item=>grid.appendChild(createCard(item)));
        section.appendChild(grid);
        content.appendChild(section);

        // nav button
        const btn=document.createElement('button');
        btn.className='type-btn';
        btn.textContent=t.name;
        btn.dataset.target = section.id;
        btn.dataset.optional = t.optional ? '1' : '0';
        btn.setAttribute('role','tab');
        btn.addEventListener('click',()=>{
          activateSection(section.id);
        });
        btnWrap.appendChild(btn);
      });

      topbar.appendChild(btnWrap);

      // åˆ‡æ¢å¯é€‰ç±»å‹æ˜¾ç¤º/éšè—
      let optionalShown = false;
      const syncOptionalVisibility = () => {
        document.querySelectorAll('[data-optional=\'1\']').forEach(el=>{
          el.classList.toggle('hidden', !optionalShown);
        });
      };
      toggleOptionalBtn.addEventListener('click', ()=>{
        optionalShown = !optionalShown;
        syncOptionalVisibility();
      });
      // åˆå§‹åŒ–ä¸€æ¬¡
      syncOptionalVisibility();

      // å†…å®¹æ ‡é¢˜ç‚¹å‡»åŒæ ·å¯æŠ˜å /å±•å¼€å¹¶å®šä½
      content.addEventListener('click', (e)=>{
        const h = e.target.closest('.type-title');
        if (!h) return;
        const targetId = h.dataset.target;
        if (targetId) activateSection(targetId);
      });

      // é»˜è®¤å±•å¼€ç¬¬ä¸€ä¸ªééšè—çš„ç±»å‹
      const firstSection = Array.from(document.querySelectorAll('.section')).find(sec => !sec.classList.contains('hidden'));
      if (firstSection) {
        activateSection(firstSection.id);
      }
    }
```

å·²å®ç°â€œå¯é€‰ç±»å‹å¼€å…³â€åŠŸèƒ½ï¼š

- åœ¨ `js/type.js` ç»™ç±»å‹å¢åŠ  `optional` å­—æ®µï¼š
  - optional: false â†’ å§‹ç»ˆæ˜¾ç¤º

- é»˜è®¤ä»…å±•å¼€ç¬¬ä¸€ä¸ªâ€œå½“å‰å¯è§â€çš„ç±»å‹ï¼›ç‚¹ä»»æ„ç±»å‹ï¼ˆé¡¶éƒ¨æˆ–å†…å®¹æ ‡é¢˜ï¼‰ä»ä¼šæŠ˜å å…¶ä»–å¹¶å¹³æ»‘å®šä½ã€‚

å¦‚éœ€è°ƒæ•´å“ªäº›æ˜¯å¯é€‰ç±»å‹ï¼Œåªéœ€åœ¨ `js/type.js` çš„ç›¸åº”é¡¹ä¸Šè®¾ç½® `optional: true/false`ã€‚

ç¤ºä¾‹ï¼ˆä»…ç¤ºæ„ä¸€é¡¹ï¼‰:
```js
// js/data/game.js
{
  title: "Steam",
  url: "https://store.steampowered.com/",
```

```html
<!DOCTYPE html>
<html lang="zh-CN">
<head>
  <meta charset="UTF-8" />
  <meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1.0" />
  <link rel="icon" type="image/png" href="favicon.png" />
  <title>æˆ‘çš„æ”¶è—å¤¹</title>
  <style>
    body {font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; margin: 0; padding: 0px 20px 20px; background:#f7f7f7;}
    h1 {text-align:left; font-size:18px; margin-bottom:24px;}
    section {margin-bottom: 40px;}
          h2 {border-left: 4px solid #3f51b5; padding-left: 8px; color:#3f51b5;}
      .type-title {cursor:pointer;}
    ul {list-style:none; padding:0;}
    li {background:#fff; margin:8px 0; padding:12px 16px; border-radius:6px; box-shadow:0 1px 3px rgba(0,0,0,.1);}  
    a {text-decoration:none; color:#333; font-weight:bold;}
    p {margin:4px 0 0; color:#666; font-size:14px;}
    /* ç½‘æ ¼å¡ç‰‡æ ·å¼ */
    .grid {display:grid; grid-template-columns:repeat(auto-fill,minmax(220px,1fr)); gap:16px; margin:16px 0;}
    .card {position:relative; display:block; height:140px; border-radius:8px; overflow:hidden; background-size:cover; background-position:center; box-shadow:0 2px 6px rgba(0,0,0,.12); transition:transform .2s; color:#fff; text-decoration:none;}
    .card:hover {transform:translateY(-4px);}
    .overlay {position:absolute; inset:0; background:rgba(0,0,0,.45); padding:10px; display:flex; flex-direction:column; justify-content:flex-end;}
    .overlay h3 {margin:0; font-size:16px;}
    .overlay p {margin:4px 0 0; font-size:12px;}
    /* é¡¶éƒ¨ç±»å‹å¯¼èˆªä¸æŠ˜å æ ·å¼ */
    .topbar {position:sticky; top:0; z-index:10; background:#fff; padding:8px 0; margin:-10px 0 12px; box-shadow:0 1px 4px rgba(0,0,0,.06);} 
    .topbar .types {display:flex; gap:8px; flex-wrap:wrap; justify-content:flex-start; padding-left:8px;}
    .type-btn {border:1px solid #ddd; background:#fafafa; color:#333; padding:6px 10px; border-radius:16px; cursor:pointer; font-size:14px;}
    .type-btn.active {background:#3f51b5; border-color:#3f51b5; color:#fff;}
    .section.collapsed .grid {display:none;}
    .hidden {display:none !important;}

    /* æ ‡é¢˜è¡Œä¸éšè”½æŒ‰é’®æ ·å¼ */
    .title-row {display:flex; align-items:center; gap:8px;}
    .title-row h1 {flex:0 0 auto;}
    .type-btn.ghost {background:transparent; border-color:transparent; color:#999; padding:4px 8px; font-size:12px;}
    .type-btn.ghost:hover {background:#f2f2f2; color:#666;}
  </style>
</head>
<body>
  <div class="title-row">
    <h1>æˆ‘çš„ç½‘ç«™æ”¶è—</h1>
    <button id="toggle-optional" class="type-btn ghost" title="å¯é€‰ç±»å‹">å¯é€‰ç±»å‹</button>
  </div>
  <nav id="topbar" class="topbar"></nav>
  <!-- å†…å®¹å®¹å™¨ -->
  <div id="content"></div>

  <!-- å¼•å…¥ç±»å‹æ˜ å°„ -->
  <script src="js/type.js"></script>

  <script>
    /*
      å‡è®¾æ¯ä¸ªæ•°æ®æ–‡ä»¶ä¸­å®šä¹‰äº†å¦‚ä¸‹æ ¼å¼çš„æ•°ç»„ï¼š
      const links = [ { title, url, description } ]
    */
  </script>

  <script>
    const loadScript = src => new Promise((res, rej) => {
      const s = document.createElement('script');
      s.src = src; s.onload = res; s.onerror = () => rej(new Error('åŠ è½½å¤±è´¥:'+src));
      document.head.appendChild(s);
    });

    function createCard(item){
      const a=document.createElement('a'); a.className='card'; a.href=item.url; a.target='_blank'; a.rel='noopener noreferrer';
      if(item.cover) a.style.backgroundImage=`url('${item.cover}')`;
      const overlay=document.createElement('div'); overlay.className='overlay'; const text = item.summary || item.description || ''; overlay.innerHTML=`<h3>${item.title}</h3><p>${text}</p>`;
      a.appendChild(overlay); return a;
    }

    function activateSection(sectionId){
      document.querySelectorAll('.type-btn').forEach(b=>{
        b.classList.toggle('active', b.dataset.target === sectionId);
      });
      document.querySelectorAll('.section').forEach(sec=>{
        sec.classList.toggle('collapsed', sec.id !== sectionId);
      });
      const target = document.getElementById(sectionId);
      if (target) {
        const topbar = document.getElementById('topbar');
        const offset = (topbar ? topbar.offsetHeight : 0) + 8; // é€‚å½“ç•™ç™½
        const y = target.getBoundingClientRect().top + window.pageYOffset - offset;
        window.scrollTo({ top: y, behavior: 'smooth' });
      }
    }

    function render(){
      const content=document.getElementById('content');
      const topbar=document.getElementById('topbar');
      const toggleOptionalBtn = document.getElementById('toggle-optional');

      // é¡¶éƒ¨æŒ‰é’®
      const btnWrap=document.createElement('div'); btnWrap.className='types';
      btnWrap.setAttribute('role','tablist');

      // å›åˆ°é¡¶éƒ¨æŒ‰é’®
      const homeBtn=document.createElement('button');
      homeBtn.className='type-btn';
      homeBtn.textContent='é¦–é¡µ';
      homeBtn.addEventListener('click',()=>{
        // æ¸…é™¤æ¿€æ´»
        document.querySelectorAll('.type-btn').forEach(b=>b.classList.remove('active'));
        // æŠ˜å æ‰€æœ‰ç±»å‹
        document.querySelectorAll('.section').forEach(sec=>sec.classList.add('collapsed'));
        // å¹³æ»‘æ»šåŠ¨åˆ°æ ‡é¢˜ä½ç½®ï¼ˆè€ƒè™‘é¡¶éƒ¨å¯¼èˆªé«˜åº¦åç§»ï¼‰
        const topbar = document.getElementById('topbar');
        const header = document.querySelector('.title-row') || document.querySelector('h1');
        const offset = (topbar ? topbar.offsetHeight : 0) + 8;
        const y = (header ? header.getBoundingClientRect().top + window.pageYOffset : 0) - offset;
        window.scrollTo({ top: y, behavior: 'smooth' });
      });
      btnWrap.appendChild(homeBtn);

      types.forEach((t, idx)=>{
        const store=window.linkStore||{}; const data=store[t.id];
        if(!Array.isArray(data) || !data.length) return;

        // section
        const section=document.createElement('section');
        section.className='section';
        section.id = `section-${t.id}`;
        section.dataset.optional = t.optional ? '1' : '0';
        section.innerHTML=`<h2 class=\"type-title\" data-target=\"section-${t.id}\">${t.name}</h2>`;
        const grid=document.createElement('div'); grid.className='grid';
        data.forEach(item=>grid.appendChild(createCard(item)));
        section.appendChild(grid);
        content.appendChild(section);

        // nav button
        const btn=document.createElement('button');
        btn.className='type-btn';
        btn.textContent=t.name;
        btn.dataset.target = section.id;
        btn.dataset.optional = t.optional ? '1' : '0';
        btn.setAttribute('role','tab');
        btn.addEventListener('click',()=>{
          activateSection(section.id);
        });
        btnWrap.appendChild(btn);
      });

      topbar.appendChild(btnWrap);

      // åˆ‡æ¢å¯é€‰ç±»å‹æ˜¾ç¤º/éšè—
      let optionalShown = false;
      const syncOptionalVisibility = () => {
        document.querySelectorAll('[data-optional=\'1\']').forEach(el=>{
          el.classList.toggle('hidden', !optionalShown);
        });
      };
      toggleOptionalBtn.addEventListener('click', ()=>{
        optionalShown = !optionalShown;
        syncOptionalVisibility();
      });
      // åˆå§‹åŒ–ä¸€æ¬¡
      syncOptionalVisibility();

      // å†…å®¹æ ‡é¢˜ç‚¹å‡»åŒæ ·å¯æŠ˜å /å±•å¼€å¹¶å®šä½
      content.addEventListener('click', (e)=>{
        const h = e.target.closest('.type-title');
        if (!h) return;
        const targetId = h.dataset.target;
        if (targetId) activateSection(targetId);
      });

      // é»˜è®¤ä¸æ»šåŠ¨åˆ°ä»»ä½•ç±»å‹ï¼Œä¿æŒåœ¨é¡¶éƒ¨
      document.querySelectorAll('.section').forEach(sec=>sec.classList.add('collapsed'));
    }

    Promise.all(types.map(t=>loadScript(t.file))).then(render).catch(console.error);
  </script>
</body>
</html>

```

```html
      const p=document.createElement('p'); p.className='summary'; p.textContent=text;
      info.appendChild(titleEl); info.appendChild(p);

    }

    function activateSection(sectionId){

        document.querySelectorAll('.type-btn').forEach(b=>b.classList.remove('active'));
        // æŠ˜å æ‰€æœ‰ç±»å‹
        document.querySelectorAll('.section').forEach(sec=>sec.classList.add('collapsed'));
        // å¹³æ»‘æ»šåŠ¨åˆ°æ ‡é¢˜ä½ç½®ï¼ˆè€ƒè™‘é¡¶éƒ¨å¯¼èˆªé«˜åº¦åç§»ï¼‰
        const topbar = document.getElementById('topbar');
        const header = document.querySelector('.title-row') || document.querySelector('h1');
        const offset = (topbar ? topbar.offsetHeight : 0) + 8;
        const y = (header ? header.getBoundingClientRect().top + window.pageYOffset : 0) - offset;
        window.scrollTo({ top: y, behavior: 'smooth' });
      });
      btnWrap.appendChild(homeBtn);

      types.forEach((t, idx)=>{
        const store=window.linkStore||{}; const data=store[t.id];
        if(!Array.isArray(data) || !data.length) return;

        // section
        const section=document.createElement('section');
        section.className='section';
        section.id = `section-${t.id}`;
        section.dataset.optional = t.optional ? '1' : '0';
        section.innerHTML=`<h2 class=\"type-title\" data-target=\"section-${t.id}\">${t.name}</h2>`;
        const grid=document.createElement('div'); grid.className='grid';
        data.forEach(item=>grid.appendChild(createCard(item)));
        section.appendChild(grid);
        content.appendChild(section);

        // nav button
        const btn=document.createElement('button');
        btn.className='type-btn';
        btn.textContent=t.name;
        btn.dataset.target = section.id;
        btn.dataset.optional = t.optional ? '1' : '0';
        btn.setAttribute('role','tab');
        btn.addEventListener('click',()=>{
          activateSection(section.id);
        });
        btnWrap.appendChild(btn);
      });

      topbar.appendChild(btnWrap);

      // åˆ‡æ¢å¯é€‰ç±»å‹æ˜¾ç¤º/éšè—
      let optionalShown = false;
      const syncOptionalVisibility = () => {
        document.querySelectorAll('[data-optional=\'1\']').forEach(el=>{
          el.classList.toggle('hidden', !optionalShown);
        });
      };
      toggleOptionalBtn.addEventListener('click', ()=>{
        optionalShown = !optionalShown;
        syncOptionalVisibility();
      });
      // åˆå§‹åŒ–ä¸€æ¬¡
      syncOptionalVisibility();

      // å†…å®¹æ ‡é¢˜ç‚¹å‡»åŒæ ·å¯æŠ˜å /å±•å¼€å¹¶å®šä½
      content.addEventListener('click', (e)=>{
        const h = e.target.closest('.type-title');
        if (!h) return;
        const targetId = h.dataset.target;
        if (targetId) activateSection(targetId);
      });

      // é»˜è®¤ä¸æ»šåŠ¨åˆ°ä»»ä½•ç±»å‹ï¼Œä¿æŒåœ¨é¡¶éƒ¨
      document.querySelectorAll('.section').forEach(sec=>sec.classList.add('collapsed'));
    }

    Promise.all(types.map(t=>loadScript(t.file))).then(render).catch(console.error);
  </script>
</body>
</html>

```

å·²æŒ‰ä½ çš„è¦æ±‚æ›´æ–°å¡ç‰‡æ ·å¼ä¸æ¸²æŸ“ï¼š

- ä¸å†ä¸Šç§»ï¼šhover æ—¶å–æ¶ˆä½ç§»ï¼Œä»…ä¿ç•™å¯é€‰çš„é˜´å½±å¢å¼ºï¼ˆå¦‚ä¸éœ€è¦å¯åˆ é™¤è¯¥è¡Œï¼‰ã€‚
- ç§»é™¤æ•´å¡åŠé€é®ç½©ï¼šæ”¹ä¸ºåº•éƒ¨æ¸å˜ä¿¡æ¯æ  `.info`ã€‚
- æ¸å˜èƒŒæ™¯æ‰¿è½½æ ‡é¢˜ä¸æ‘˜è¦ï¼šæ ‡é¢˜ `.info .title` ä¸æ‘˜è¦ `.info .summary` æ”¾åœ¨æ¸å˜æ å†…ã€‚
- æ‘˜è¦ä¸¤è¡Œï¼š`.info .summary` é€šè¿‡ `-webkit-line-clamp: 2` é™åˆ¶æ˜¾ç¤ºä¸¤è¡Œï¼Œè¶…å‡ºçœç•¥ã€‚
- ç•™å‡ºå¯è°ƒé¡¹ä½ç½®ï¼š
  - æ ‡é¢˜è¡Œè·ä¸é¢œè‰²ï¼š`.info .title { line-height / color }`
  - æ‘˜è¦è¡Œè·ä¸é¢œè‰²ï¼š`.info .summary { line-height / color }`

ä½ å¯ä»¥ç›´æ¥åœ¨ `index.html` çš„ä¸Šè¿° CSS é€‰æ‹©å™¨å¤„è°ƒèŠ‚è¡Œé—´è·ä¸å­—è‰²ã€‚

**User**

ä¿®æ”¹1. å¡ç‰‡ä¸Šsummaryçš„å†…å®¹å¦‚æœè¶…è¿‡ä¸€è¡Œï¼Œè¶…å‡ºçš„éƒ¨åˆ†å˜æˆäº†...ï¼Œ æˆ‘å¸Œæœ›èƒ½å¤Ÿæ¢è¡Œåˆ°ç¬¬äºŒè¡Œï¼Œè¶…å‡ºç¬¬äºŒè¡Œçš„èŒƒå›´å†æ˜¾ç¤º...ï¼Œ 2. åº•éƒ¨æ¸å˜ä¿¡æ¯æ çš„é€æ˜åº¦å˜åŒ–æ¢ä¸€ç§æ›²çº¿ï¼Œä¸Šç¼“ä¸‹æ€¥ï¼Œä½¿ç”¨linearå¤ªå¹³ç¼“äº†

---

**Cursor**

I'll update the styles in index.html to:
- Ensure summary wraps to a second line before clamping (remove single-line ellipsis, add white-space and word-break).
- Adjust the gradient of the bottom info bar using multiple color stops to create an "ease-out" effect (ä¸Šç¼“ä¸‹æ€¥).
Proceeding to edit the CSS.

```html
<!DOCTYPE html>
<html lang="zh-CN">
<head>
  <meta charset="UTF-8" />
  <meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1.0" />
  <link rel="icon" type="image/png" href="favicon.png" />
  <title>æˆ‘çš„æ”¶è—å¤¹</title>
  <style>
    body {font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; margin: 0; padding: 0px 20px 20px; background:#f7f7f7;}
    h1 {text-align:left; font-size:18px; margin-bottom:24px;}
    section {margin-bottom: 40px;}
          h2 {border-left: 4px solid #3f51b5; padding-left: 8px; color:#3f51b5;}
      .type-title {cursor:pointer;}
    ul {list-style:none; padding:0;}
    li {background:#fff; margin:8px 0; padding:12px 16px; border-radius:6px; box-shadow:0 1px 3px rgba(0,0,0,.1);}  
    a {text-decoration:none; color:#333; font-weight:bold;}
    p {margin:4px 0 0; color:#666; font-size:14px;}
    /* ç½‘æ ¼å¡ç‰‡æ ·å¼ */
    .grid {display:grid; grid-template-columns:repeat(auto-fill,minmax(220px,1fr)); gap:16px; margin:16px 0;}
    .card {position:relative; display:block; height:140px; border-radius:8px; overflow:hidden; background-size:cover; background-position:center; box-shadow:0 2px 6px rgba(0,0,0,.12); transition:box-shadow .2s; color:#fff; text-decoration:none;}
    /* 1) æ‚¬åœæ—¶å¡ç‰‡ä¸ç§»åŠ¨ï¼Œä»…å¾®è°ƒé˜´å½±ï¼ˆå¦‚ä¸éœ€è¦å¯åˆ é™¤ä¸‹ä¸€è¡Œï¼‰ */
    .card:hover {transform:none; box-shadow:0 4px 12px rgba(0,0,0,.18);} 
    /* 2) å»é™¤æ•´å¡åŠé€é®ç½©ï¼Œæ”¹ä¸ºåº•éƒ¨æ¸å˜ä¿¡æ¯æ  */
    /* 2) åº•éƒ¨æ¸å˜ä¿¡æ¯æ ï¼šä¸Šç¼“ä¸‹æ€¥ï¼ˆå¤šæ®µè‰²æ ‡æ¨¡æ‹Ÿéçº¿æ€§è¿‡æ¸¡ï¼‰ */
    .info {position:absolute; left:0; right:0; bottom:0; padding:10px; background:linear-gradient(to top,
      rgba(0,0,0,.75) 0%,
      rgba(0,0,0,.60) 35%,
      rgba(0,0,0,.30) 70%,
      rgba(0,0,0,0) 100%
    );}
    /* 5) æ ‡æ³¨: å¯åœ¨æ­¤è°ƒæ•´æ ‡é¢˜é¢œè‰²ä¸è¡Œè· */
    .info .title {margin:0; font-size:16px; line-height:1.2; color:#ffffff;}
    /* 4) summary æ˜¾ç¤ºä¸¤è¡Œï¼Œå¹¶å¯åœ¨æ­¤è°ƒæ•´é¢œè‰²ä¸è¡Œè· */
    .info .summary {margin:4px 0 0; font-size:12px; line-height:1.4; color:rgba(255,255,255,.9);
      /* è®©å†…å®¹å…ˆè‡ªç„¶æ¢è¡Œåˆ°ç¬¬äºŒè¡Œï¼Œè¶…å‡ºç¬¬äºŒè¡Œå†çœç•¥ */
      white-space: normal; word-break: break-word; overflow: hidden;
      display: -webkit-box; -webkit-box-orient: vertical; -webkit-line-clamp: 2;
    }
    /* é¡¶éƒ¨ç±»å‹å¯¼èˆªä¸æŠ˜å æ ·å¼ */
    .topbar {position:sticky; top:0; z-index:10; background:#fff; padding:8px 0; margin:-10px 0 12px; box-shadow:0 1px 4px rgba(0,0,0,.06);}

    .section.collapsed .grid {display:none;}
    .hidden {display:none !important;}

    .title-row h1 {flex:0 0 auto;}
    .type-btn.ghost {background:transparent; border-color:transparent; color:#999; padding:4px 8px; font-size:12px;}
    .type-btn.ghost:hover {background:#f2f2f2; color:#666;}

<body>
  <div class="title-row">
    <h1>æˆ‘çš„ç½‘ç«™æ”¶è—</h1>
    <button id="toggle-optional" class="type-btn ghost" title="å¯é€‰ç±»å‹">å¯é€‰ç±»å‹</button>
  </div>
  <nav id="topbar" class="topbar"></nav>
  <!-- å†…å®¹å®¹å™¨ -->
  <div id="content"></div>

  <!-- å¼•å…¥ç±»å‹æ˜ å°„ -->
  <script src="js/type.js"></script>

  <script>
    /*
      å‡è®¾æ¯ä¸ªæ•°æ®æ–‡ä»¶ä¸­å®šä¹‰äº†å¦‚ä¸‹æ ¼å¼çš„æ•°ç»„ï¼š
      const links = [ { title, url, description } ]
    */
  </script>

  <script>
    const loadScript = src => new Promise((res, rej) => {
      const s = document.createElement('script');
      s.src = src; s.onload = res; s.onerror = () => rej(new Error('åŠ è½½å¤±è´¥:'+src));
      document.head.appendChild(s);
    });

    function createCard(item){
      const a=document.createElement('a'); a.className='card'; a.href=item.url; a.target='_blank'; a.rel='noopener noreferrer';
      if(item.cover) a.style.backgroundImage=`url('${item.cover}')`;
      const info=document.createElement('div'); info.className='info';
      const titleEl=document.createElement('h3'); titleEl.className='title'; titleEl.textContent=item.title;
      const text = item.summary || item.description || '';
      const p=document.createElement('p'); p.className='summary'; p.textContent=text;
      info.appendChild(titleEl); info.appendChild(p);
      a.appendChild(info); return a;
    }

    function activateSection(sectionId){
      document.querySelectorAll('.type-btn').forEach(b=>{
        b.classList.toggle('active', b.dataset.target === sectionId);
      });
      document.querySelectorAll('.section').forEach(sec=>{
        sec.classList.toggle('collapsed', sec.id !== sectionId);
      });
      const target = document.getElementById(sectionId);
      if (target) {
        const topbar = document.getElementById('topbar');
        const offset = (topbar ? topbar.offsetHeight : 0) + 8; // é€‚å½“ç•™ç™½
        const y = target.getBoundingClientRect().top + window.pageYOffset - offset;
        window.scrollTo({ top: y, behavior: 'smooth' });
      }
    }

    function render(){
      const content=document.getElementById('content');
      const topbar=document.getElementById('topbar');
      const toggleOptionalBtn = document.getElementById('toggle-optional');

      // é¡¶éƒ¨æŒ‰é’®
      const btnWrap=document.createElement('div'); btnWrap.className='types';
      btnWrap.setAttribute('role','tablist');

      // å›åˆ°é¡¶éƒ¨æŒ‰é’®
      const homeBtn=document.createElement('button');
      homeBtn.className='type-btn';
      homeBtn.textContent='é¦–é¡µ';
      homeBtn.addEventListener('click',()=>{
        // æ¸…é™¤æ¿€æ´»
        document.querySelectorAll('.type-btn').forEach(b=>b.classList.remove('active'));
        // æŠ˜å æ‰€æœ‰ç±»å‹
        document.querySelectorAll('.section').forEach(sec=>sec.classList.add('collapsed'));
        // å¹³æ»‘æ»šåŠ¨åˆ°æ ‡é¢˜ä½ç½®ï¼ˆè€ƒè™‘é¡¶éƒ¨å¯¼èˆªé«˜åº¦åç§»ï¼‰
        const topbar = document.getElementById('topbar');
        const header = document.querySelector('.title-row') || document.querySelector('h1');
        const offset = (topbar ? topbar.offsetHeight : 0) + 8;
        const y = (header ? header.getBoundingClientRect().top + window.pageYOffset : 0) - offset;
        window.scrollTo({ top: y, behavior: 'smooth' });
      });
      btnWrap.appendChild(homeBtn);

      types.forEach((t, idx)=>{
        const store=window.linkStore||{}; const data=store[t.id];
        if(!Array.isArray(data) || !data.length) return;

        // section
        const section=document.createElement('section');
        section.className='section';
        section.id = `section-${t.id}`;
        section.dataset.optional = t.optional ? '1' : '0';
        section.innerHTML=`<h2 class=\"type-title\" data-target=\"section-${t.id}\">${t.name}</h2>`;
        const grid=document.createElement('div'); grid.className='grid';
        data.forEach(item=>grid.appendChild(createCard(item)));
        section.appendChild(grid);
        content.appendChild(section);

        // nav button
        const btn=document.createElement('button');
        btn.className='type-btn';
        btn.textContent=t.name;
        btn.dataset.target = section.id;
        btn.dataset.optional = t.optional ? '1' : '0';
        btn.setAttribute('role','tab');
        btn.addEventListener('click',()=>{
          activateSection(section.id);
        });
        btnWrap.appendChild(btn);
      });

      topbar.appendChild(btnWrap);

      // åˆ‡æ¢å¯é€‰ç±»å‹æ˜¾ç¤º/éšè—
      let optionalShown = false;
      const syncOptionalVisibility = () => {
        document.querySelectorAll('[data-optional=\'1\']').forEach(el=>{
          el.classList.toggle('hidden', !optionalShown);
        });
      };
      toggleOptionalBtn.addEventListener('click', ()=>{
        optionalShown = !optionalShown;
        syncOptionalVisibility();
      });
      // åˆå§‹åŒ–ä¸€æ¬¡
      syncOptionalVisibility();

      // å†…å®¹æ ‡é¢˜ç‚¹å‡»åŒæ ·å¯æŠ˜å /å±•å¼€å¹¶å®šä½
      content.addEventListener('click', (e)=>{
        const h = e.target.closest('.type-title');
        if (!h) return;
        const targetId = h.dataset.target;
        if (targetId) activateSection(targetId);
      });

      // é»˜è®¤ä¸æ»šåŠ¨åˆ°ä»»ä½•ç±»å‹ï¼Œä¿æŒåœ¨é¡¶éƒ¨
      document.querySelectorAll('.section').forEach(sec=>sec.classList.add('collapsed'));
    }

    Promise.all(types.map(t=>loadScript(t.file))).then(render).catch(console.error);
  </script>
</body>
</html>
```

å·²è°ƒæ•´å®Œæˆï¼š
- summary ç°åœ¨ä¼šè‡ªç„¶æ¢è¡Œåˆ°ç¬¬äºŒè¡Œï¼Œåªæœ‰è¶…è¿‡ç¬¬äºŒè¡Œçš„éƒ¨åˆ†æ‰è¢«æˆªæ–­çœç•¥ï¼ˆä¿ç•™ä¸¤è¡Œæ˜¾ç¤ºï¼‰ã€‚
- åº•éƒ¨ä¿¡æ¯æ çš„æ¸å˜æ”¹ä¸ºå¤šæ®µè‰²æ ‡ï¼Œå½¢æˆâ€œä¸Šç¼“ä¸‹æ€¥â€çš„è¿‡æ¸¡æ•ˆæœï¼Œæ›´è´´è¿‘ ease-out çš„è§‚æ„Ÿã€‚

è‹¥éœ€æ›´æŸ”æˆ–æ›´å¼ºçš„è¿‡æ¸¡ï¼Œå¯åœ¨ `.info` çš„ `linear-gradient` ä¸­å¾®è°ƒæ¯ä¸ªä¸é€æ˜åº¦ä¸ç™¾åˆ†æ¯”ï¼›è‹¥éœ€æ›´ç´§å‡‘æˆ–æ›´ç–æ¾çš„è¡Œè·/å­—è‰²ï¼Œå¯åœ¨ `.info .summary` ä¸ `.info .title` é‡Œè°ƒæ•´ `line-height` ä¸ `color`ã€‚

```html
    /* 1) æ‚¬åœæ—¶å¡ç‰‡ä¸ç§»åŠ¨ï¼Œä»…å¾®è°ƒé˜´å½±ï¼ˆå¦‚ä¸éœ€è¦å¯åˆ é™¤ä¸‹ä¸€è¡Œï¼‰ */
    .card:hover {transform:none; box-shadow:0 4px 12px rgba(0,0,0,.18);} 
    /* 2) å»é™¤æ•´å¡åŠé€é®ç½©ï¼Œæ”¹ä¸ºåº•éƒ¨æ¸å˜ä¿¡æ¯æ  */
    /* 2) åº•éƒ¨æ¸å˜ä¿¡æ¯æ ï¼šä¸Šç¼“ä¸‹æ€¥ï¼ˆå¤šæ®µè‰²æ ‡æ¨¡æ‹Ÿéçº¿æ€§è¿‡æ¸¡ï¼‰ */
    .info {position:absolute; left:0; right:0; bottom:0; padding:10px; background:linear-gradient(to top,
      rgba(0,0,0,.75) 0%,
      rgba(0,0,0,.60) 35%,
      rgba(0,0,0,.30) 70%,
      rgba(0,0,0,0) 100%
    ); transition: top .25s ease, padding .25s ease;}
    /* æ‚¬åœæ—¶ï¼Œä¿¡æ¯æ æ‰©å±•åˆ°æ•´å¼ å¡ç‰‡ */
    .card:hover .info {top:0;}
    /* å åŠ ä¸€ä¸ªå¯åŠ¨ç”»çš„åŠé€æ˜èƒŒæ™¯å±‚ */
    .info::before {content:""; position:absolute; inset:0; background:rgba(0,0,0,.6); opacity:0; transition:opacity .25s ease;}
    .card:hover .info::before {opacity:1;}
    /* æ–‡æœ¬ç½®äºåŠé€æ˜å±‚ä¹‹ä¸Š */
    .info > * {position:relative; z-index:1;}
    /* 5) æ ‡æ³¨: å¯åœ¨æ­¤è°ƒæ•´æ ‡é¢˜é¢œè‰²ä¸è¡Œè· */
    .info .title {margin:0; font-size:16px; line-height:1.2; color:#ffffff;}
    /* 4) summary æ˜¾ç¤ºä¸¤è¡Œï¼Œå¹¶å¯åœ¨æ­¤è°ƒæ•´é¢œè‰²ä¸è¡Œè· */
    .info .summary {margin:4px 0 0; font-size:12px; line-height:1.4; color:rgba(255,255,255,.9);
      /* è®©å†…å®¹å…ˆè‡ªç„¶æ¢è¡Œåˆ°ç¬¬äºŒè¡Œï¼Œè¶…å‡ºç¬¬äºŒè¡Œå†çœç•¥ */
      white-space: normal; word-break: break-word; overflow: hidden;
      display: -webkit-box; -webkit-box-orient: vertical; -webkit-line-clamp: 2;
    }
    /* hover æ—¶æ˜¾ç¤ºæ›´è¯¦ç»†æè¿°ï¼Œéšè— summary */
    .info .desc {display:none; margin:6px 0 0; font-size:12px; line-height:1.5; color:rgba(255,255,255,.95);} /* å¯è°ƒé¢œè‰²ä¸è¡Œè· */
    .card:hover .info .desc {display:block;}
    .card:hover .info .summary {display:none;}
    /* é¡¶éƒ¨ç±»å‹å¯¼èˆªä¸æŠ˜å æ ·å¼ */
    .topbar {position:sticky; top:0; z-index:10; background:#fff; padding:8px 0; margin:-10px 0 12px; box-shadow:0 1px 4px rgba(0,0,0,.06);} 
    .topbar .types {display:flex; gap:8px; flex-wrap:wrap; justify-content:flex-start; padding-left:8px;}
    .type-btn {border:1px solid #ddd; background:#fafafa; color:#333; padding:6px 10px; border-radius:16px; cursor:pointer; font-size:14px;}
    .type-btn.active {background:#3f51b5; border-color:#3f51b5; color:#fff;}
    .section.collapsed .grid {display:none;}
    .hidden {display:none !important;}

    /* æ ‡é¢˜è¡Œä¸éšè”½æŒ‰é’®æ ·å¼ */
    .title-row {display:flex; align-items:center; gap:8px;}
    .title-row h1 {flex:0 0 auto;}
    .type-btn.ghost {background:transparent; border-color:transparent; color:#999; padding:4px 8px; font-size:12px;}
    .type-btn.ghost:hover {background:#f2f2f2; color:#666;}
  </style>
</head>
<body>
  <div class="title-row">
    <h1>æˆ‘çš„ç½‘ç«™æ”¶è—</h1>
    <button id="toggle-optional" class="type-btn ghost" title="å¯é€‰ç±»å‹">å¯é€‰ç±»å‹</button>
  </div>
  <nav id="topbar" class="topbar"></nav>
  <!-- å†…å®¹å®¹å™¨ -->
  <div id="content"></div>

  <!-- å¼•å…¥ç±»å‹æ˜ å°„ -->
  <script src="js/type.js"></script>

  <script>
    /*
      å‡è®¾æ¯ä¸ªæ•°æ®æ–‡ä»¶ä¸­å®šä¹‰äº†å¦‚ä¸‹æ ¼å¼çš„æ•°ç»„ï¼š
      const links = [ { title, url, description } ]
    */
  </script>

  <script>
    const loadScript = src => new Promise((res, rej) => {
      const s = document.createElement('script');
      s.src = src; s.onload = res; s.onerror = () => rej(new Error('åŠ è½½å¤±è´¥:'+src));
      document.head.appendChild(s);
    });

    function createCard(item){
      const a=document.createElement('a'); a.className='card'; a.href=item.url; a.target='_blank'; a.rel='noopener noreferrer';
      if(item.cover) a.style.backgroundImage=`url('${item.cover}')`;
      const info=document.createElement('div'); info.className='info';
      const titleEl=document.createElement('h3'); titleEl.className='title'; titleEl.textContent=item.title;
      const text = item.summary || item.description || '';
      const p=document.createElement('p'); p.className='summary'; p.textContent=text;
      info.appendChild(titleEl); info.appendChild(p);
```
```html
      a.appendChild(info); return a;
    }

    function activateSection(sectionId){
      document.querySelectorAll('.type-btn').forEach(b=>{
        b.classList.toggle('active', b.dataset.target === sectionId);
      });
      document.querySelectorAll('.section').forEach(sec=>{
        sec.classList.toggle('collapsed', sec.id !== sectionId);
      });
      const target = document.getElementById(sectionId);
      if (target) {
        const topbar = document.getElementById('topbar');
        const offset = (topbar ? topbar.offsetHeight : 0) + 8; // é€‚å½“ç•™ç™½
        const y = target.getBoundingClientRect().top + window.pageYOffset - offset;
        window.scrollTo({ top: y, behavior: 'smooth' });
      }
    }

    function render(){
      const content=document.getElementById('content');
      const topbar=document.getElementById('topbar');
      const toggleOptionalBtn = document.getElementById('toggle-optional');

      // é¡¶éƒ¨æŒ‰é’®
      const btnWrap=document.createElement('div'); btnWrap.className='types';
      btnWrap.setAttribute('role','tablist');

      // å›åˆ°é¡¶éƒ¨æŒ‰é’®
      const homeBtn=document.createElement('button');
      homeBtn.className='type-btn';
      homeBtn.textContent='é¦–é¡µ';
      homeBtn.addEventListener('click',()=>{
        // æ¸…é™¤æ¿€æ´»
        document.querySelectorAll('.type-btn').forEach(b=>b.classList.remove('active'));
        // æŠ˜å æ‰€æœ‰ç±»å‹
        document.querySelectorAll('.section').forEach(sec=>sec.classList.add('collapsed'));
        // å¹³æ»‘æ»šåŠ¨åˆ°æ ‡é¢˜ä½ç½®ï¼ˆè€ƒè™‘é¡¶éƒ¨å¯¼èˆªé«˜åº¦åç§»ï¼‰
        const topbar = document.getElementById('topbar');
        const header = document.querySelector('.title-row') || document.querySelector('h1');
        const offset = (topbar ? topbar.offsetHeight : 0) + 8;
        const y = (header ? header.getBoundingClientRect().top + window.pageYOffset : 0) - offset;
        window.scrollTo({ top: y, behavior: 'smooth' });
      });
      btnWrap.appendChild(homeBtn);

      types.forEach((t, idx)=>{
        const store=window.linkStore||{}; const data=store[t.id];
        if(!Array.isArray(data) || !data.length) return;

        // section
        const section=document.createElement('section');
        section.className='section';
        section.id = `section-${t.id}`;
        section.dataset.optional = t.optional ? '1' : '0';
        section.innerHTML=`<h2 class=\"type-title\" data-target=\"section-${t.id}\">${t.name}</h2>`;
        const grid=document.createElement('div'); grid.className='grid';
        data.forEach(item=>grid.appendChild(createCard(item)));
        section.appendChild(grid);
        content.appendChild(section);

        // nav button
        const btn=document.createElement('button');
        btn.className='type-btn';
        btn.textContent=t.name;
        btn.dataset.target = section.id;
        btn.dataset.optional = t.optional ? '1' : '0';
        btn.setAttribute('role','tab');
        btn.addEventListener('click',()=>{
          activateSection(section.id);
        });
        btnWrap.appendChild(btn);
      });

      topbar.appendChild(btnWrap);

      // åˆ‡æ¢å¯é€‰ç±»å‹æ˜¾ç¤º/éšè—
      let optionalShown = false;
      const syncOptionalVisibility = () => {
        document.querySelectorAll('[data-optional=\'1\']').forEach(el=>{
          el.classList.toggle('hidden', !optionalShown);
        });
      };
      toggleOptionalBtn.addEventListener('click', ()=>{
        optionalShown = !optionalShown;
        syncOptionalVisibility();
      });
      // åˆå§‹åŒ–ä¸€æ¬¡
      syncOptionalVisibility();

      // å†…å®¹æ ‡é¢˜ç‚¹å‡»åŒæ ·å¯æŠ˜å /å±•å¼€å¹¶å®šä½
      content.addEventListener('click', (e)=>{
        const h = e.target.closest('.type-title');
        if (!h) return;
        const targetId = h.dataset.target;
        if (targetId) activateSection(targetId);
      });

      // é»˜è®¤ä¸æ»šåŠ¨åˆ°ä»»ä½•ç±»å‹ï¼Œä¿æŒåœ¨é¡¶éƒ¨
      document.querySelectorAll('.section').forEach(sec=>sec.classList.add('collapsed'));
    }

    Promise.all(types.map(t=>loadScript(t.file))).then(render).catch(console.error);
  </script>
</body>
</html>

```

å·²å®ç°æ–°çš„ hover æ•ˆæœï¼š
- é¼ æ ‡ç§»å…¥å¡ç‰‡æ—¶ï¼Œåº•éƒ¨ä¿¡æ¯æ å¹³æ»‘å±•å¼€ä¸ºè¦†ç›–æ•´å¼ å¡ç‰‡çš„åŠé€æ˜èƒŒæ™¯ï¼ˆå¸¦åŠ¨ç”»ï¼‰ã€‚
- å±•å¼€çŠ¶æ€æ˜¾ç¤ºæ ‡é¢˜ä¸â€œè¯¦ç»†æè¿°â€ï¼ˆdescriptionï¼‰ï¼Œéšè—ä¸¤è¡Œæ‘˜è¦ï¼ˆsummaryï¼‰ã€‚
- é¼ æ ‡ç§»å‡ºæ—¶æ¢å¤ä¸ºåº•éƒ¨æ¸å˜ä¿¡æ¯æ ï¼Œä»…æ˜¾ç¤ºæ ‡é¢˜ä¸ä¸¤è¡Œæ‘˜è¦ã€‚

å¦‚éœ€è°ƒæ•´é€æ˜åº¦ä¸åŠ¨ç”»ï¼š
- è¦†ç›–å±‚é€æ˜åº¦/åŠ¨ç”»ï¼š`.info::before { background / opacity / transition }`
- æ¸å˜å¼ºåº¦ä¸èŠ‚å¥ï¼š`.info { background: linear-gradient(...) }`
- æ ‡é¢˜ã€æ‘˜è¦ã€æè¿°çš„è¡Œè·ä¸å­—è‰²ï¼š`.info .title`ã€`.info .summary`ã€`.info .desc`

---

**User**

For the code present, we get this error:
```
Also define the standard property 'line-clamp' for compatibility
```
How can I resolve this? If you propose a fix, please make it concise.

---

**Cursor**

I'll add the standard CSS property alongside the prefixed one to satisfy the linter by updating the `.info .summary` rule to include `line-clamp: 2;`.

```html
<!DOCTYPE html>
<html lang="zh-CN">
<head>
  <meta charset="UTF-8" />
  <meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1.0" />

  <style>

          h2 {border-left: 4px solid #3f51b5; padding-left: 8px; color:#3f51b5;}

    .card:hover {transform:none; box-shadow:0 4px 12px rgba(0,0,0,.18);}

    .info {position:absolute; left:0; right:0; bottom:0; padding:10px; background:linear-gradient(to top,
      rgba(0,0,0,.75) 0%,

    ); transition: top .25s ease, padding .25s ease;}

    .card:hover .info::before {opacity:1;}
    /* æ–‡æœ¬ç½®äºåŠé€æ˜å±‚ä¹‹ä¸Š */
    .info > * {position:relative; z-index:1;}
    /* 5) æ ‡æ³¨: å¯åœ¨æ­¤è°ƒæ•´æ ‡é¢˜é¢œè‰²ä¸è¡Œè· */
    .info .title {margin:0; font-size:16px; line-height:1.2; color:#ffffff;}
    /* 4) summary æ˜¾ç¤ºä¸¤è¡Œï¼Œå¹¶å¯åœ¨æ­¤è°ƒæ•´é¢œè‰²ä¸è¡Œè· */
    .info .summary {margin:4px 0 0; font-size:12px; line-height:1.4; color:rgba(255,255,255,.9);
      /* è®©å†…å®¹å…ˆè‡ªç„¶æ¢è¡Œåˆ°ç¬¬äºŒè¡Œï¼Œè¶…å‡ºç¬¬äºŒè¡Œå†çœç•¥ */
      white-space: normal; word-break: break-word; overflow: hidden;
      display: -webkit-box; -webkit-box-orient: vertical; -webkit-line-clamp: 2; line-clamp: 2;
    }
    /* hover æ—¶æ˜¾ç¤ºæ›´è¯¦ç»†æè¿°ï¼Œéšè— summary */
    .info .desc {display:none; margin:6px 0 0; font-size:12px; line-height:1.5; color:rgba(255,255,255,.95);} /* å¯è°ƒé¢œè‰²ä¸è¡Œè· */
    .card:hover .info .desc {display:block;}
    .card:hover .info .summary {display:none;}
    /* é¡¶éƒ¨ç±»å‹å¯¼èˆªä¸æŠ˜å æ ·å¼ */
    .topbar {position:sticky; top:0; z-index:10; background:#fff; padding:8px 0; margin:-10px 0 12px; box-shadow:0 1px 4px rgba(0,0,0,.06);} 
    .topbar .types {display:flex; gap:8px; flex-wrap:wrap; justify-content:flex-start; padding-left:8px;}
    .type-btn {border:1px solid #ddd; background:#fafafa; color:#333; padding:6px 10px; border-radius:16px; cursor:pointer; font-size:14px;}
    .type-btn.active {background:#3f51b5; border-color:#3f51b5; color:#fff;}
    .section.collapsed .grid {display:none;}
    .hidden {display:none !important;}

    /* æ ‡é¢˜è¡Œä¸éšè”½æŒ‰é’®æ ·å¼ */
    .title-row {display:flex; align-items:center; gap:8px;}
    .title-row h1 {flex:0 0 auto;}
    .type-btn.ghost {background:transparent; border-color:transparent; color:#999; padding:4px 8px; font-size:12px;}
    .type-btn.ghost:hover {background:#f2f2f2; color:#666;}
  </style>
</head>
<body>
  <div class="title-row">
    <h1>æˆ‘çš„ç½‘ç«™æ”¶è—</h1>
    <button id="toggle-optional" class="type-btn ghost" title="å¯é€‰ç±»å‹">å¯é€‰ç±»å‹</button>
  </div>
  <nav id="topbar" class="topbar"></nav>
  <!-- å†…å®¹å®¹å™¨ -->
  <div id="content"></div>

  <!-- å¼•å…¥ç±»å‹æ˜ å°„ -->
  <script src="js/type.js"></script>

  <script>
    /*
      å‡è®¾æ¯ä¸ªæ•°æ®æ–‡ä»¶ä¸­å®šä¹‰äº†å¦‚ä¸‹æ ¼å¼çš„æ•°ç»„ï¼š
      const links = [ { title, url, description } ]
    */
  </script>

  <script>
    const loadScript = src => new Promise((res, rej) => {
      const s = document.createElement('script');
      s.src = src; s.onload = res; s.onerror = () => rej(new Error('åŠ è½½å¤±è´¥:'+src));
      document.head.appendChild(s);
    });

    function createCard(item){
      const a=document.createElement('a'); a.className='card'; a.href=item.url; a.target='_blank'; a.rel='noopener noreferrer';
      if(item.cover) a.style.backgroundImage=`url('${item.cover}')`;
      const info=document.createElement('div'); info.className='info';
      const titleEl=document.createElement('h3'); titleEl.className='title'; titleEl.textContent=item.title;
      const text = item.summary || item.description || '';
      const p=document.createElement('p'); p.className='summary'; p.textContent=text;
      const desc=document.createElement('p'); desc.className='desc'; desc.textContent=item.description || '';
      info.appendChild(titleEl); info.appendChild(p); info.appendChild(desc);
      a.appendChild(info); return a;
    }

    function activateSection(sectionId){
      document.querySelectorAll('.type-btn').forEach(b=>{
        b.classList.toggle('active', b.dataset.target === sectionId);
      });
      document.querySelectorAll('.section').forEach(sec=>{
        sec.classList.toggle('collapsed', sec.id !== sectionId);
      });
      const target = document.getElementById(sectionId);
      if (target) {
        const topbar = document.getElementById('topbar');
        const offset = (topbar ? topbar.offsetHeight : 0) + 8; // é€‚å½“ç•™ç™½
        const y = target.getBoundingClientRect().top + window.pageYOffset - offset;
        window.scrollTo({ top: y, behavior: 'smooth' });
      }
    }

    function render(){
      const content=document.getElementById('content');
      const topbar=document.getElementById('topbar');
      const toggleOptionalBtn = document.getElementById('toggle-optional');

      // é¡¶éƒ¨æŒ‰é’®
      const btnWrap=document.createElement('div'); btnWrap.className='types';
      btnWrap.setAttribute('role','tablist');

      // å›åˆ°é¡¶éƒ¨æŒ‰é’®
      const homeBtn=document.createElement('button');
      homeBtn.className='type-btn';
      homeBtn.textContent='é¦–é¡µ';
      homeBtn.addEventListener('click',()=>{
        // æ¸…é™¤æ¿€æ´»
        document.querySelectorAll('.type-btn').forEach(b=>b.classList.remove('active'));
        // æŠ˜å æ‰€æœ‰ç±»å‹
        document.querySelectorAll('.section').forEach(sec=>sec.classList.add('collapsed'));
        // å¹³æ»‘æ»šåŠ¨åˆ°æ ‡é¢˜ä½ç½®ï¼ˆè€ƒè™‘é¡¶éƒ¨å¯¼èˆªé«˜åº¦åç§»ï¼‰
        const topbar = document.getElementById('topbar');
        const header = document.querySelector('.title-row') || document.querySelector('h1');
        const offset = (topbar ? topbar.offsetHeight : 0) + 8;
        const y = (header ? header.getBoundingClientRect().top + window.pageYOffset : 0) - offset;
        window.scrollTo({ top: y, behavior: 'smooth' });
      });
      btnWrap.appendChild(homeBtn);

      types.forEach((t, idx)=>{
        const store=window.linkStore||{}; const data=store[t.id];
        if(!Array.isArray(data) || !data.length) return;

        // section
        const section=document.createElement('section');
        section.className='section';
        section.id = `section-${t.id}`;
        section.dataset.optional = t.optional ? '1' : '0';
        section.innerHTML=`<h2 class=\"type-title\" data-target=\"section-${t.id}\">${t.name}</h2>`;
        const grid=document.createElement('div'); grid.className='grid';
        data.forEach(item=>grid.appendChild(createCard(item)));
        section.appendChild(grid);
        content.appendChild(section);

        // nav button
        const btn=document.createElement('button');
        btn.className='type-btn';
        btn.textContent=t.name;
        btn.dataset.target = section.id;
        btn.dataset.optional = t.optional ? '1' : '0';
        btn.setAttribute('role','tab');
        btn.addEventListener('click',()=>{
          activateSection(section.id);
        });
        btnWrap.appendChild(btn);
      });

      topbar.appendChild(btnWrap);

      // åˆ‡æ¢å¯é€‰ç±»å‹æ˜¾ç¤º/éšè—
      let optionalShown = false;
      const syncOptionalVisibility = () => {
        document.querySelectorAll('[data-optional=\'1\']').forEach(el=>{
          el.classList.toggle('hidden', !optionalShown);
        });
      };
      toggleOptionalBtn.addEventListener('click', ()=>{
        optionalShown = !optionalShown;
        syncOptionalVisibility();
      });
      // åˆå§‹åŒ–ä¸€æ¬¡
      syncOptionalVisibility();

      // å†…å®¹æ ‡é¢˜ç‚¹å‡»åŒæ ·å¯æŠ˜å /å±•å¼€å¹¶å®šä½
      content.addEventListener('click', (e)=>{
        const h = e.target.closest('.type-title');
        if (!h) return;
        const targetId = h.dataset.target;
        if (targetId) activateSection(targetId);
      });

      // é»˜è®¤ä¸æ»šåŠ¨åˆ°ä»»ä½•ç±»å‹ï¼Œä¿æŒåœ¨é¡¶éƒ¨
      document.querySelectorAll('.section').forEach(sec=>sec.classList.add('collapsed'));
    }

    Promise.all(types.map(t=>loadScript(t.file))).then(render).catch(console.error);
  </script>
</body>
</html>

```

- Add the standard property next to the prefixed one:
```css
.info .summary {
  /* ... */
  display: -webkit-box;
  -webkit-box-orient: vertical;
  -webkit-line-clamp: 2;
  line-clamp: 2; /* standard */
}
```
- Keep both for widest compatibility and to satisfy the linter.

```css
.info .summary {
  /* ... */
  display: -webkit-box;
  -webkit-box-orient: vertical;
  -webkit-line-clamp: 2;
  line-clamp: 2; /* standard */
}
```

---

**User**

å°†æŒ‰é’®â€œå¯é€‰ç±»å‹â€æ”¹æˆä¸€ä¸ªè¾“å…¥æ¡†ï¼Œå½“è¾“å…¥â€œ72875â€å¹¶æŒ‰ä¸‹å›è½¦æˆ–è€…ç‚¹å‡»æœç´¢æ—¶ï¼Œæ˜¾ç¤ºéšè—ç±»å‹ï¼Œå½“è¾“å…¥â€œ0â€å¹¶æŒ‰ä¸‹å›è½¦æˆ–è€…ç‚¹å‡»æœç´¢æ—¶æ˜¾ç¤ºé»˜è®¤çš„ç±»å‹ï¼Œè¾“å…¥æ¡†è¦æ”¾åœ¨â€œæˆ‘çš„ç½‘ç«™æ”¶è—â€è¿™ä¸€è¡Œï¼Œå³å¯¹é½å¹¶æµå‡ºé€‚å½“ç©ºç™½

---

**Cursor**

I'll place a right-aligned input and search button next to the title, then update the script to toggle optional types when the user enters 72875 (show) or 0 (default) via Enter or clicking search. Proceeding to update index.html.

```html
    /* æ–‡æœ¬ç½®äºåŠé€æ˜å±‚ä¹‹ä¸Š */

    /* 5) æ ‡æ³¨: å¯åœ¨æ­¤è°ƒæ•´æ ‡é¢˜é¢œè‰²ä¸è¡Œè· */

    /* 4) summary æ˜¾ç¤ºä¸¤è¡Œï¼Œå¹¶å¯åœ¨æ­¤è°ƒæ•´é¢œè‰²ä¸è¡Œè· */
    .info .summary {margin:4px 0 0; font-size:12px; line-height:1.4; color:rgba(255,255,255,.9);
      /* è®©å†…å®¹å…ˆè‡ªç„¶æ¢è¡Œåˆ°ç¬¬äºŒè¡Œï¼Œè¶…å‡ºç¬¬äºŒè¡Œå†çœç•¥ */
      white-space: normal; word-break: break-word; overflow: hidden;

    .card:hover .info .summary {display:none;}

  <div class="title-row">
    <h1>æˆ‘çš„ç½‘ç«™æ”¶è—</h1>
    <div class="action-right">

    function activateSection(sectionId){

        b.classList.toggle('active', b.dataset.target === sectionId);
      });

      });

        const topbar = document.getElementById('topbar');
        const offset = (topbar ? topbar.offsetHeight : 0) + 8; // é€‚å½“ç•™ç™½
        const y = target.getBoundingClientRect().top + window.pageYOffset - offset;
        window.scrollTo({ top: y, behavior: 'smooth' });
      }
    }

    function render(){
      const content=document.getElementById('content');
      const topbar=document.getElementById('topbar');
      const toggleOptionalBtn = document.getElementById('toggle-optional');

      // é¡¶éƒ¨æŒ‰é’®
      const btnWrap=document.createElement('div'); btnWrap.className='types';
      btnWrap.setAttribute('role','tablist');

      // å›åˆ°é¡¶éƒ¨æŒ‰é’®
      const homeBtn=document.createElement('button');
      homeBtn.className='type-btn';
      homeBtn.textContent='é¦–é¡µ';
      homeBtn.addEventListener('click',()=>{
        // æ¸…é™¤æ¿€æ´»
        document.querySelectorAll('.type-btn').forEach(b=>b.classList.remove('active'));
        // æŠ˜å æ‰€æœ‰ç±»å‹
        document.querySelectorAll('.section').forEach(sec=>sec.classList.add('collapsed'));
        // å¹³æ»‘æ»šåŠ¨åˆ°æ ‡é¢˜ä½ç½®ï¼ˆè€ƒè™‘é¡¶éƒ¨å¯¼èˆªé«˜åº¦åç§»ï¼‰
        const topbar = document.getElementById('topbar');
        const header = document.querySelector('.title-row') || document.querySelector('h1');
        const offset = (topbar ? topbar.offsetHeight : 0) + 8;
        const y = (header ? header.getBoundingClientRect().top + window.pageYOffset : 0) - offset;
        window.scrollTo({ top: y, behavior: 'smooth' });
      });
      btnWrap.appendChild(homeBtn);

      types.forEach((t, idx)=>{
        const store=window.linkStore||{}; const data=store[t.id];
        if(!Array.isArray(data) || !data.length) return;

        // section
        const section=document.createElement('section');
        section.className='section';
        section.id = `section-${t.id}`;
        section.dataset.optional = t.optional ? '1' : '0';

          activateSection(section.id);
        });
        btnWrap.appendChild(btn);
      });

      topbar.appendChild(btnWrap);

      // åˆ‡æ¢å¯é€‰ç±»å‹æ˜¾ç¤º/éšè—
      let optionalShown = false;
      const syncOptionalVisibility = () => {
        document.querySelectorAll('[data-optional=\'1\']').forEach(el=>{
          el.classList.toggle('hidden', !optionalShown);
        });
      };
      toggleOptionalBtn.addEventListener('click', ()=>{
        optionalShown = !optionalShown;
        syncOptionalVisibility();
      });
      // åˆå§‹åŒ–ä¸€æ¬¡
      syncOptionalVisibility();

      // å†…å®¹æ ‡é¢˜ç‚¹å‡»åŒæ ·å¯æŠ˜å /å±•å¼€å¹¶å®šä½
      content.addEventListener('click', (e)=>{
        const h = e.target.closest('.type-title');
        if (!h) return;
        const targetId = h.dataset.target;
        if (targetId) activateSection(targetId);
      });

      // é»˜è®¤ä¸æ»šåŠ¨åˆ°ä»»ä½•ç±»å‹ï¼Œä¿æŒåœ¨é¡¶éƒ¨
      document.querySelectorAll('.section').forEach(sec=>sec.classList.add('collapsed'));
    }

    Promise.all(types.map(t=>loadScript(t.file))).then(render).catch(console.error);
  </script>
</body>
```

```html
<!DOCTYPE html>
<html lang="zh-CN">
<head>
  <meta charset="UTF-8" />
  <meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1.0" />
  <link rel="icon" type="image/png" href="favicon.png" />

  <style>
    body {font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; margin: 0; padding: 0px 20px 20px; background:#f7f7f7;}
    h1 {text-align:left; font-size:18px; margin-bottom:24px;}

          h2 {border-left: 4px solid #3f51b5; padding-left: 8px; color:#3f51b5;}
      .type-title {cursor:pointer;}
    ul {list-style:none; padding:0;}
    li {background:#fff; margin:8px 0; padding:12px 16px; border-radius:6px; box-shadow:0 1px 3px rgba(0,0,0,.1);}  
    a {text-decoration:none; color:#333; font-weight:bold;}
    p {margin:4px 0 0; color:#666; font-size:14px;}
    /* ç½‘æ ¼å¡ç‰‡æ ·å¼ */
    .grid {display:grid; grid-template-columns:repeat(auto-fill,minmax(220px,1fr)); gap:16px; margin:16px 0;}
    .card {position:relative; display:block; height:140px; border-radius:8px; overflow:hidden; background-size:cover; background-position:center; box-shadow:0 2px 6px rgba(0,0,0,.12); transition:box-shadow .2s; color:#fff; text-decoration:none;}
    /* 1) æ‚¬åœæ—¶å¡ç‰‡ä¸ç§»åŠ¨ï¼Œä»…å¾®è°ƒé˜´å½±ï¼ˆå¦‚ä¸éœ€è¦å¯åˆ é™¤ä¸‹ä¸€è¡Œï¼‰ */
    .card:hover {transform:none; box-shadow:0 4px 12px rgba(0,0,0,.18);} 
    /* 2) å»é™¤æ•´å¡åŠé€é®ç½©ï¼Œæ”¹ä¸ºåº•éƒ¨æ¸å˜ä¿¡æ¯æ  */
    /* 2) åº•éƒ¨æ¸å˜ä¿¡æ¯æ ï¼šä¸Šç¼“ä¸‹æ€¥ï¼ˆå¤šæ®µè‰²æ ‡æ¨¡æ‹Ÿéçº¿æ€§è¿‡æ¸¡ï¼‰ */
    .info {position:absolute; left:0; right:0; bottom:0; padding:10px; background:linear-gradient(to top,
      rgba(0,0,0,.75) 0%,
      rgba(0,0,0,.60) 35%,
      rgba(0,0,0,.30) 70%,
      rgba(0,0,0,0) 100%
    ); transition: top .25s ease, padding .25s ease;}
    /* æ‚¬åœæ—¶ï¼Œä¿¡æ¯æ æ‰©å±•åˆ°æ•´å¼ å¡ç‰‡ */
    .card:hover .info {top:0;}
    /* å åŠ ä¸€ä¸ªå¯åŠ¨ç”»çš„åŠé€æ˜èƒŒæ™¯å±‚ */
    .info::before {content:""; position:absolute; inset:0; background:rgba(0,0,0,.6); opacity:0; transition:opacity .25s ease;}
    .card:hover .info::before {opacity:1;}
    /* æ–‡æœ¬ç½®äºåŠé€æ˜å±‚ä¹‹ä¸Š */
    .info > * {position:relative; z-index:1;}
    /* 5) æ ‡æ³¨: å¯åœ¨æ­¤è°ƒæ•´æ ‡é¢˜é¢œè‰²ä¸è¡Œè· */
    .info .title {margin:0; font-size:16px; line-height:1.2; color:#ffffff;}
    /* 4) summary æ˜¾ç¤ºä¸¤è¡Œï¼Œå¹¶å¯åœ¨æ­¤è°ƒæ•´é¢œè‰²ä¸è¡Œè· */
    .info .summary {margin:4px 0 0; font-size:12px; line-height:1.4; color:rgba(255,255,255,.9);
      /* è®©å†…å®¹å…ˆè‡ªç„¶æ¢è¡Œåˆ°ç¬¬äºŒè¡Œï¼Œè¶…å‡ºç¬¬äºŒè¡Œå†çœç•¥ */
      white-space: normal; word-break: break-word; overflow: hidden;
      display: -webkit-box; -webkit-box-orient: vertical; -webkit-line-clamp: 2; line-clamp: 2;
    }
    /* hover æ—¶æ˜¾ç¤ºæ›´è¯¦ç»†æè¿°ï¼Œéšè— summary */
    .info .desc {display:none; margin:6px 0 0; font-size:12px; line-height:1.5; color:rgba(255,255,255,.95);} /* å¯è°ƒé¢œè‰²ä¸è¡Œè· */
    .card:hover .info .desc {display:block;}
    .card:hover .info .summary {display:none;}
    /* é¡¶éƒ¨ç±»å‹å¯¼èˆªä¸æŠ˜å æ ·å¼ */
    .topbar {position:sticky; top:0; z-index:10; background:#fff; padding:8px 0; margin:-10px 0 12px; box-shadow:0 1px 4px rgba(0,0,0,.06);} 
    .topbar .types {display:flex; gap:8px; flex-wrap:wrap; justify-content:flex-start; padding-left:8px;}
    .type-btn {border:1px solid #ddd; background:#fafafa; color:#333; padding:6px 10px; border-radius:16px; cursor:pointer; font-size:14px;}
    .type-btn.active {background:#3f51b5; border-color:#3f51b5; color:#fff;}
    .section.collapsed .grid {display:none;}
    .hidden {display:none !important;}

    /* æ ‡é¢˜è¡Œä¸éšè”½æŒ‰é’®æ ·å¼ */
    .title-row {display:flex; align-items:center; gap:8px;}
    .title-row h1 {flex:1 1 auto;}
    .action-right {flex:0 0 auto; display:flex; align-items:center; gap:6px;}
    .search-input {height:28px; padding:0 8px; border:1px solid #ddd; border-radius:14px; font-size:12px; width:140px;}
    .type-btn.ghost {background:transparent; border-color:transparent; color:#999; padding:4px 8px; font-size:12px;}
    .type-btn.ghost:hover {background:#f2f2f2; color:#666;}
  </style>
</head>
<body>
  <div class="title-row">
    <h1>æˆ‘çš„ç½‘ç«™æ”¶è—</h1>
    <div class="action-right">
      <input id="optional-key" class="search-input" placeholder="è¾“å…¥å£ä»¤" />
      <button id="optional-search" class="type-btn ghost" title="æœç´¢">æœç´¢</button>
    </div>
  </div>
  <nav id="topbar" class="topbar"></nav>
  <!-- å†…å®¹å®¹å™¨ -->
  <div id="content"></div>

  <!-- å¼•å…¥ç±»å‹æ˜ å°„ -->
  <script src="js/type.js"></script>

  <script>
    /*
      å‡è®¾æ¯ä¸ªæ•°æ®æ–‡ä»¶ä¸­å®šä¹‰äº†å¦‚ä¸‹æ ¼å¼çš„æ•°ç»„ï¼š
      const links = [ { title, url, description } ]
    */
  </script>

  <script>
    const loadScript = src => new Promise((res, rej) => {
      const s = document.createElement('script');
      s.src = src; s.onload = res; s.onerror = () => rej(new Error('åŠ è½½å¤±è´¥:'+src));
      document.head.appendChild(s);
    });

    function createCard(item){
      const a=document.createElement('a'); a.className='card'; a.href=item.url; a.target='_blank'; a.rel='noopener noreferrer';
      if(item.cover) a.style.backgroundImage=`url('${item.cover}')`;
      const info=document.createElement('div'); info.className='info';
      const titleEl=document.createElement('h3'); titleEl.className='title'; titleEl.textContent=item.title;
      const text = item.summary || item.description || '';
      const p=document.createElement('p'); p.className='summary'; p.textContent=text;
      const desc=document.createElement('p'); desc.className='desc'; desc.textContent=item.description || '';
      info.appendChild(titleEl); info.appendChild(p); info.appendChild(desc);
      a.appendChild(info); return a;
    }

    function activateSection(sectionId){
      document.querySelectorAll('.type-btn').forEach(b=>{
        b.classList.toggle('active', b.dataset.target === sectionId);
      });
      document.querySelectorAll('.section').forEach(sec=>{
        sec.classList.toggle('collapsed', sec.id !== sectionId);
      });
      const target = document.getElementById(sectionId);
      if (target) {
        const topbar = document.getElementById('topbar');
        const offset = (topbar ? topbar.offsetHeight : 0) + 8; // é€‚å½“ç•™ç™½
        const y = target.getBoundingClientRect().top + window.pageYOffset - offset;
        window.scrollTo({ top: y, behavior: 'smooth' });
      }
    }

    function render(){
      const content=document.getElementById('content');
      const topbar=document.getElementById('topbar');
      const toggleOptionalBtn = document.getElementById('toggle-optional');

      // é¡¶éƒ¨æŒ‰é’®
      const btnWrap=document.createElement('div'); btnWrap.className='types';
      btnWrap.setAttribute('role','tablist');

      // å›åˆ°é¡¶éƒ¨æŒ‰é’®
      const homeBtn=document.createElement('button');
      homeBtn.className='type-btn';
      homeBtn.textContent='é¦–é¡µ';
      homeBtn.addEventListener('click',()=>{
        // æ¸…é™¤æ¿€æ´»
        document.querySelectorAll('.type-btn').forEach(b=>b.classList.remove('active'));
        // æŠ˜å æ‰€æœ‰ç±»å‹
        document.querySelectorAll('.section').forEach(sec=>sec.classList.add('collapsed'));
        // å¹³æ»‘æ»šåŠ¨åˆ°æ ‡é¢˜ä½ç½®ï¼ˆè€ƒè™‘é¡¶éƒ¨å¯¼èˆªé«˜åº¦åç§»ï¼‰
        const topbar = document.getElementById('topbar');
        const header = document.querySelector('.title-row') || document.querySelector('h1');
        const offset = (topbar ? topbar.offsetHeight : 0) + 8;
        const y = (header ? header.getBoundingClientRect().top + window.pageYOffset : 0) - offset;
        window.scrollTo({ top: y, behavior: 'smooth' });
      });
      btnWrap.appendChild(homeBtn);

      types.forEach((t, idx)=>{
        const store=window.linkStore||{}; const data=store[t.id];
        if(!Array.isArray(data) || !data.length) return;

        // section
        const section=document.createElement('section');
        section.className='section';
        section.id = `section-${t.id}`;
        section.dataset.optional = t.optional ? '1' : '0';
        section.innerHTML=`<h2 class=\"type-title\" data-target=\"section-${t.id}\">${t.name}</h2>`;
        const grid=document.createElement('div'); grid.className='grid';
        data.forEach(item=>grid.appendChild(createCard(item)));
        section.appendChild(grid);
        content.appendChild(section);

        // nav button
        const btn=document.createElement('button');
        btn.className='type-btn';
        btn.textContent=t.name;
        btn.dataset.target = section.id;
        btn.dataset.optional = t.optional ? '1' : '0';
        btn.setAttribute('role','tab');
        btn.addEventListener('click',()=>{
          activateSection(section.id);
        });
        btnWrap.appendChild(btn);
      });

      topbar.appendChild(btnWrap);

      // åˆ‡æ¢å¯é€‰ç±»å‹æ˜¾ç¤º/éšè—
      let optionalShown = false;
      const syncOptionalVisibility = () => {
        document.querySelectorAll('[data-optional=\'1\']').forEach(el=>{
          el.classList.toggle('hidden', !optionalShown);
        });
      };
      toggleOptionalBtn.addEventListener('click', ()=>{
        optionalShown = !optionalShown;
        syncOptionalVisibility();
      });
      // åˆå§‹åŒ–ä¸€æ¬¡
      syncOptionalVisibility();

      // å†…å®¹æ ‡é¢˜ç‚¹å‡»åŒæ ·å¯æŠ˜å /å±•å¼€å¹¶å®šä½
      content.addEventListener('click', (e)=>{
        const h = e.target.closest('.type-title');
        if (!h) return;
        const targetId = h.dataset.target;
        if (targetId) activateSection(targetId);
      });

      // é»˜è®¤ä¸æ»šåŠ¨åˆ°ä»»ä½•ç±»å‹ï¼Œä¿æŒåœ¨é¡¶éƒ¨
      document.querySelectorAll('.section').forEach(sec=>sec.classList.add('collapsed'));
    }

    Promise.all(types.map(t=>loadScript(t.file))).then(render).catch(console.error);
  </script>
</body>
</html>
```

```html
    /* 5) æ ‡æ³¨: å¯åœ¨æ­¤è°ƒæ•´æ ‡é¢˜é¢œè‰²ä¸è¡Œè· */

      /* è®©å†…å®¹å…ˆè‡ªç„¶æ¢è¡Œåˆ°ç¬¬äºŒè¡Œï¼Œè¶…å‡ºç¬¬äºŒè¡Œå†çœç•¥ */

    </div>
  </div>
  <nav id="topbar" class="topbar"></nav>
  <!-- å†…å®¹å®¹å™¨ -->
  <div id="content"></div>

  <!-- å¼•å…¥ç±»å‹æ˜ å°„ -->

  <script>
    /*
      å‡è®¾æ¯ä¸ªæ•°æ®æ–‡ä»¶ä¸­å®šä¹‰äº†å¦‚ä¸‹æ ¼å¼çš„æ•°ç»„ï¼š
      const links = [ { title, url, description } ]
    */
  </script>

  <script>
    const loadScript = src => new Promise((res, rej) => {
      const s = document.createElement('script');
      s.src = src; s.onload = res; s.onerror = () => rej(new Error('åŠ è½½å¤±è´¥:'+src));
      document.head.appendChild(s);
    });

    function createCard(item){
      const a=document.createElement('a'); a.className='card'; a.href=item.url; a.target='_blank'; a.rel='noopener noreferrer';
      if(item.cover) a.style.backgroundImage=`url('${item.cover}')`;
      const info=document.createElement('div'); info.className='info';
      const titleEl=document.createElement('h3'); titleEl.className='title'; titleEl.textContent=item.title;
      const text = item.summary || item.description || '';
      const p=document.createElement('p'); p.className='summary'; p.textContent=text;
      const desc=document.createElement('p'); desc.className='desc'; desc.textContent=item.description || '';
      info.appendChild(titleEl); info.appendChild(p); info.appendChild(desc);
      a.appendChild(info); return a;
    }

    function activateSection(sectionId){
      document.querySelectorAll('.type-btn').forEach(b=>{
        b.classList.toggle('active', b.dataset.target === sectionId);
      });
      document.querySelectorAll('.section').forEach(sec=>{
        sec.classList.toggle('collapsed', sec.id !== sectionId);
      });
      const target = document.getElementById(sectionId);
      if (target) {
        const topbar = document.getElementById('topbar');
        const offset = (topbar ? topbar.offsetHeight : 0) + 8; // é€‚å½“ç•™ç™½
        const y = target.getBoundingClientRect().top + window.pageYOffset - offset;
        window.scrollTo({ top: y, behavior: 'smooth' });
      }
    }

    function render(){
      const content=document.getElementById('content');
      const topbar=document.getElementById('topbar');
      const input = document.getElementById('optional-key');
      const searchBtn = document.getElementById('optional-search');

      // é¡¶éƒ¨æŒ‰é’®
      const btnWrap=document.createElement('div'); btnWrap.className='types';
      btnWrap.setAttribute('role','tablist');

      // å›åˆ°é¡¶éƒ¨æŒ‰é’®
      const homeBtn=document.createElement('button');
      homeBtn.className='type-btn';
      homeBtn.textContent='é¦–é¡µ';
      homeBtn.addEventListener('click',()=>{
        // æ¸…é™¤æ¿€æ´»
        document.querySelectorAll('.type-btn').forEach(b=>b.classList.remove('active'));
        // æŠ˜å æ‰€æœ‰ç±»å‹
        document.querySelectorAll('.section').forEach(sec=>sec.classList.add('collapsed'));
        // å¹³æ»‘æ»šåŠ¨åˆ°æ ‡é¢˜ä½ç½®ï¼ˆè€ƒè™‘é¡¶éƒ¨å¯¼èˆªé«˜åº¦åç§»ï¼‰
        const topbar = document.getElementById('topbar');
        const header = document.querySelector('.title-row') || document.querySelector('h1');
        const offset = (topbar ? topbar.offsetHeight : 0) + 8;
        const y = (header ? header.getBoundingClientRect().top + window.pageYOffset : 0) - offset;
        window.scrollTo({ top: y, behavior: 'smooth' });
      });
      btnWrap.appendChild(homeBtn);

      types.forEach((t, idx)=>{
        const store=window.linkStore||{}; const data=store[t.id];
        if(!Array.isArray(data) || !data.length) return;

        // section
        const section=document.createElement('section');
        section.className='section';
        section.id = `section-${t.id}`;
        section.dataset.optional = t.optional ? '1' : '0';
        section.innerHTML=`<h2 class=\"type-title\" data-target=\"section-${t.id}\">${t.name}</h2>`;
        const grid=document.createElement('div'); grid.className='grid';
        data.forEach(item=>grid.appendChild(createCard(item)));
        section.appendChild(grid);
        content.appendChild(section);

        // nav button
        const btn=document.createElement('button');
        btn.className='type-btn';
        btn.textContent=t.name;
        btn.dataset.target = section.id;
        btn.dataset.optional = t.optional ? '1' : '0';
        btn.setAttribute('role','tab');
        btn.addEventListener('click',()=>{
          activateSection(section.id);
        });
        btnWrap.appendChild(btn);
      });

      topbar.appendChild(btnWrap);

      // åˆ‡æ¢å¯é€‰ç±»å‹æ˜¾ç¤º/éšè—
      let optionalShown = false;
      const syncOptionalVisibility = () => {
        document.querySelectorAll('[data-optional=\'1\']').forEach(el=>{
          el.classList.toggle('hidden', !optionalShown);
        });
      };
      function handleSearch(){
        const v = (input.value || '').trim();
        if (v === '72875') { optionalShown = true; syncOptionalVisibility(); }
        else if (v === '0') { optionalShown = false; syncOptionalVisibility(); }
      }
      searchBtn.addEventListener('click', handleSearch);
      input.addEventListener('keydown', (e)=>{ if (e.key === 'Enter') handleSearch(); });
      // åˆå§‹åŒ–ä¸€æ¬¡
      syncOptionalVisibility();

      // å†…å®¹æ ‡é¢˜ç‚¹å‡»åŒæ ·å¯æŠ˜å /å±•å¼€å¹¶å®šä½
      content.addEventListener('click', (e)=>{
        const h = e.target.closest('.type-title');
        if (!h) return;
        const targetId = h.dataset.target;
        if (targetId) activateSection(targetId);
      });

      // é»˜è®¤ä¸æ»šåŠ¨åˆ°ä»»ä½•ç±»å‹ï¼Œä¿æŒåœ¨é¡¶éƒ¨
      document.querySelectorAll('.section').forEach(sec=>sec.classList.add('collapsed'));
    }

    Promise.all(types.map(t=>loadScript(t.file))).then(render).catch(console.error);
  </script>
</body>
```
