
å·²æ”¹ä¸ºè¾“å…¥æ¡†æ§åˆ¶ï¼š
- ä½ç½®ä¸æ ·å¼ï¼šåœ¨â€œæˆ‘çš„ç½‘ç«™æ”¶è—â€å³ä¾§åŠ å…¥è¾“å…¥æ¡†å’Œâ€œæœç´¢â€æŒ‰é’®ï¼Œå³å¯¹é½å¹¶ç•™å‡ºç©ºç™½ã€‚
- è¡Œä¸ºï¼š
  - è¾“å…¥ 72875 å¹¶å›è½¦æˆ–ç‚¹â€œæœç´¢â€ â†’ æ˜¾ç¤ºå¯é€‰ç±»å‹
  - è¾“å…¥ 0 å¹¶å›è½¦æˆ–ç‚¹â€œæœç´¢â€ â†’ æ¢å¤é»˜è®¤ï¼Œéšè—å¯é€‰ç±»å‹
- åŸâ€œå¯é€‰ç±»å‹â€æŒ‰é’®å·²ç§»é™¤ï¼Œé€»è¾‘å·²å…³è”åˆ°è¾“å…¥æ¡†ä¸æŒ‰é’®ã€‚

---

**User**

å°†è¿™ä¸ªç½‘ç«™ç¾åŒ–ä¸€ä¸‹ï¼Œä¿æŒæ•´ä½“é£æ ¼ç»Ÿä¸€ï¼Œçœ‹èµ·æ¥æ¯”è¾ƒèˆ’æœæ”¾æ¾çš„é¢œè‰²å’Œé£æ ¼

---

**Cursor**

I'll introduce a design token section with CSS variables, wrap the header/nav/content in a centered container, and retheme buttons, inputs, topbar, headings, and cards for a relaxed unified look without changing behavior. Now updating index.html styles and minimal markup.

```html
<!DOCTYPE html>
<html lang="zh-CN">
<head>
  <meta charset="UTF-8" />
  <meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1.0" />
  <link rel="icon" type="image/png" href="favicon.png" />
  <title>æˆ‘çš„æ”¶è—å¤¹</title>
  <style>
    :root {
      --bg: #f5f7fb;
      --surface: #ffffff;
      --surface-rgb: 255,255,255;
      --text: #2f3440;
      --muted: #6b7280;
      --border: #e6e8ee;
      --accent: #5b8def;
      --accent-600: #3f73e8;
      --shadow: 0 2px 6px rgba(0,0,0,.08);
      --shadow-lg: 0 10px 24px rgba(0,0,0,.12);
      --radius: 12px;
    }
    body {font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; margin: 0; padding: 0; background: var(--bg); color: var(--text);}    
    .page {max-width: 1100px; margin: 0 auto; padding: 0 20px 24px;}
    h1 {text-align:left; font-size:18px; margin-bottom:24px; color: var(--text);}    
    section {margin-bottom: 40px;}
          h2 {border-left: 4px solid var(--accent); padding-left: 8px; color: var(--accent);}
      .type-title {cursor:pointer;}
    ul {list-style:none; padding:0;}
    li {background:#fff; margin:8px 0; padding:12px 16px; border-radius:6px; box-shadow:0 1px 3px rgba(0,0,0,.1);}  
    a {text-decoration:none; color:#333; font-weight:bold;}
    p {margin:4px 0 0; color:#666; font-size:14px;}
    /* ç½‘æ ¼å¡ç‰‡æ ·å¼ */
    .grid {display:grid; grid-template-columns:repeat(auto-fill,minmax(220px,1fr)); gap:16px; margin:16px 0;}
    .card {position:relative; display:block; height:160px; border-radius: var(--radius); overflow:hidden; background-size:cover; background-position:center; box-shadow: var(--shadow); transition:box-shadow .2s; color:#fff; text-decoration:none;}
    /* 1) æ‚¬åœæ—¶å¡ç‰‡ä¸ç§»åŠ¨ï¼Œä»…å¾®è°ƒé˜´å½±ï¼ˆå¦‚ä¸éœ€è¦å¯åˆ é™¤ä¸‹ä¸€è¡Œï¼‰ */
    .card:hover {transform:none; box-shadow:0 4px 12px rgba(0,0,0,.18);} 
    /* 2) å»é™¤æ•´å¡åŠé€é®ç½©ï¼Œæ”¹ä¸ºåº•éƒ¨æ¸å˜ä¿¡æ¯æ  */
    /* 2) åº•éƒ¨æ¸å˜ä¿¡æ¯æ ï¼šä¸Šç¼“ä¸‹æ€¥ï¼ˆå¤šæ®µè‰²æ ‡æ¨¡æ‹Ÿéçº¿æ€§è¿‡æ¸¡ï¼‰ */
    .info {position:absolute; left:0; right:0; bottom:0; padding:10px; background:linear-gradient(to top,
      rgba(0,0,0,.75) 0%,
      rgba(0,0,0,.60) 35%,
      rgba(0,0,0,.30) 70%,
      rgba(0,0,0,0) 100%
    ); transition: top .25s ease, padding .25s ease;}
    /* æ‚¬åœæ—¶ï¼Œä¿¡æ¯æ æ‰©å±•åˆ°æ•´å¼ å¡ç‰‡ */
    .card:hover .info {top:0;}
    /* å åŠ ä¸€ä¸ªå¯åŠ¨ç”»çš„åŠé€æ˜èƒŒæ™¯å±‚ */
    .info::before {content:""; position:absolute; inset:0; background:rgba(0,0,0,.6); opacity:0; transition:opacity .25s ease;}
    .card:hover .info::before {opacity:1;}
    /* æ–‡æœ¬ç½®äºåŠé€æ˜å±‚ä¹‹ä¸Š */
    .info > * {position:relative; z-index:1;}
    /* 5) æ ‡æ³¨: å¯åœ¨æ­¤è°ƒæ•´æ ‡é¢˜é¢œè‰²ä¸è¡Œè· */
    .info .title {margin:0; font-size:16px; line-height:1.2; color:#ffffff;}
    /* 4) summary æ˜¾ç¤ºä¸¤è¡Œï¼Œå¹¶å¯åœ¨æ­¤è°ƒæ•´é¢œè‰²ä¸è¡Œè· */
    .info .summary {margin:4px 0 0; font-size:12px; line-height:1.4; color:rgba(255,255,255,.9);
      /* è®©å†…å®¹å…ˆè‡ªç„¶æ¢è¡Œåˆ°ç¬¬äºŒè¡Œï¼Œè¶…å‡ºç¬¬äºŒè¡Œå†çœç•¥ */
      white-space: normal; word-break: break-word; overflow: hidden;
      display: -webkit-box; -webkit-box-orient: vertical; -webkit-line-clamp: 2; line-clamp: 2;
    }
    /* hover æ—¶æ˜¾ç¤ºæ›´è¯¦ç»†æè¿°ï¼Œéšè— summary */
    .info .desc {display:none; margin:6px 0 0; font-size:12px; line-height:1.5; color:rgba(255,255,255,.95);} /* å¯è°ƒé¢œè‰²ä¸è¡Œè· */
    .card:hover .info .desc {display:block;}
    .card:hover .info .summary {display:none;}
    /* é¡¶éƒ¨ç±»å‹å¯¼èˆªä¸æŠ˜å æ ·å¼ */
    .topbar {position:sticky; top:0; z-index:10; background: rgba(var(--surface-rgb), .9); padding:8px 0; margin:0 0 12px; box-shadow:0 1px 4px rgba(0,0,0,.06); backdrop-filter: saturate(140%) blur(8px);} 
    .topbar .types {display:flex; gap:8px; flex-wrap:wrap; justify-content:flex-start; padding-left:8px;}
    .type-btn {border:1px solid var(--border); background: var(--surface); color: var(--text); padding:6px 12px; border-radius:999px; cursor:pointer; font-size:13px; transition:background .2s, color .2s, border-color .2s, box-shadow .2s;}
    .type-btn:hover {background:#f3f6ff; border-color:#d5def8;}
    .type-btn.active {background: var(--accent); border-color: var(--accent); color:#fff; box-shadow: 0 4px 12px rgba(91,141,239,.3);}    
    .section.collapsed .grid {display:none;}
    .hidden {display:none !important;}

    /* æ ‡é¢˜è¡Œä¸éšè”½æŒ‰é’®æ ·å¼ */
    .title-row {display:flex; align-items:center; gap:8px; padding-top: 10px;}
    .title-row h1 {flex:1 1 auto;}
    .action-right {flex:0 0 auto; display:flex; align-items:center; gap:6px;}
    .search-input {height:30px; padding:0 10px; border:1px solid var(--border); border-radius:16px; font-size:12px; width:160px; background: var(--surface); color: var(--text); transition:border-color .2s, box-shadow .2s;}
    .search-input:focus {outline:none; border-color:#c7d2fe; box-shadow:0 0 0 3px rgba(91,141,239,.18);}    
    .type-btn.ghost {background:transparent; border-color:var(--border); color:var(--muted); padding:6px 10px; font-size:12px; border-radius:999px;}
    .type-btn.ghost:hover {background:#f6f8ff; color:#55617c;}
  </style>
</head>
<body>
  <div class="title-row">
    <h1>æˆ‘çš„ç½‘ç«™æ”¶è—</h1>
    <div class="action-right">
      <input id="optional-key" class="search-input" placeholder="è¾“å…¥" />
      <button id="optional-search" class="type-btn ghost" title="æœç´¢">æœç´¢</button>
    </div>
  </div>
  <nav id="topbar" class="topbar"></nav>
  <!-- å†…å®¹å®¹å™¨ -->
  <div id="content"></div>

  <!-- å¼•å…¥ç±»å‹æ˜ å°„ -->
  <script src="js/type.js"></script>

  <script>
    /*
      å‡è®¾æ¯ä¸ªæ•°æ®æ–‡ä»¶ä¸­å®šä¹‰äº†å¦‚ä¸‹æ ¼å¼çš„æ•°ç»„ï¼š
      const links = [ { title, url, description } ]
    */
  </script>

  <script>
    const loadScript = src => new Promise((res, rej) => {
      const s = document.createElement('script');
      s.src = src; s.onload = res; s.onerror = () => rej(new Error('åŠ è½½å¤±è´¥:'+src));
      document.head.appendChild(s);
    });

    function createCard(item){
      const a=document.createElement('a'); a.className='card'; a.href=item.url; a.target='_blank'; a.rel='noopener noreferrer';
      if(item.cover) a.style.backgroundImage=`url('${item.cover}')`;
      const info=document.createElement('div'); info.className='info';
      const titleEl=document.createElement('h3'); titleEl.className='title'; titleEl.textContent=item.title;
      const text = item.summary || item.description || '';
      const p=document.createElement('p'); p.className='summary'; p.textContent=text;
      const desc=document.createElement('p'); desc.className='desc'; desc.textContent=item.description || '';
      info.appendChild(titleEl); info.appendChild(p); info.appendChild(desc);
      a.appendChild(info); return a;
    }

    function activateSection(sectionId){
      document.querySelectorAll('.type-btn').forEach(b=>{
        b.classList.toggle('active', b.dataset.target === sectionId);
      });
      document.querySelectorAll('.section').forEach(sec=>{
        sec.classList.toggle('collapsed', sec.id !== sectionId);
      });
      const target = document.getElementById(sectionId);
      if (target) {
        const topbar = document.getElementById('topbar');
        const offset = (topbar ? topbar.offsetHeight : 0) + 8; // é€‚å½“ç•™ç™½
        const y = target.getBoundingClientRect().top + window.pageYOffset - offset;
        window.scrollTo({ top: y, behavior: 'smooth' });
      }
    }

    function render(){
      const content=document.getElementById('content');
      const topbar=document.getElementById('topbar');
      const input = document.getElementById('optional-key');
      const searchBtn = document.getElementById('optional-search');

      // é¡¶éƒ¨æŒ‰é’®
      const btnWrap=document.createElement('div'); btnWrap.className='types';
      btnWrap.setAttribute('role','tablist');

      // å›åˆ°é¡¶éƒ¨æŒ‰é’®
      const homeBtn=document.createElement('button');
      homeBtn.className='type-btn';
      homeBtn.textContent='é¦–é¡µ';
      homeBtn.addEventListener('click',()=>{
        // æ¸…é™¤æ¿€æ´»
        document.querySelectorAll('.type-btn').forEach(b=>b.classList.remove('active'));
        // æŠ˜å æ‰€æœ‰ç±»å‹
        document.querySelectorAll('.section').forEach(sec=>sec.classList.add('collapsed'));
        // å¹³æ»‘æ»šåŠ¨åˆ°æ ‡é¢˜ä½ç½®ï¼ˆè€ƒè™‘é¡¶éƒ¨å¯¼èˆªé«˜åº¦åç§»ï¼‰
        const topbar = document.getElementById('topbar');
        const header = document.querySelector('.title-row') || document.querySelector('h1');
        const offset = (topbar ? topbar.offsetHeight : 0) + 8;
        const y = (header ? header.getBoundingClientRect().top + window.pageYOffset : 0) - offset;
        window.scrollTo({ top: y, behavior: 'smooth' });
      });
      btnWrap.appendChild(homeBtn);

      types.forEach((t, idx)=>{
        const store=window.linkStore||{}; const data=store[t.id];
        if(!Array.isArray(data) || !data.length) return;

        // section
        const section=document.createElement('section');
        section.className='section';
        section.id = `section-${t.id}`;
        section.dataset.optional = t.optional ? '1' : '0';
        section.innerHTML=`<h2 class=\"type-title\" data-target=\"section-${t.id}\">${t.name}</h2>`;
        const grid=document.createElement('div'); grid.className='grid';
        data.forEach(item=>grid.appendChild(createCard(item)));
        section.appendChild(grid);
        content.appendChild(section);

        // nav button
        const btn=document.createElement('button');
        btn.className='type-btn';
        btn.textContent=t.name;
        btn.dataset.target = section.id;
        btn.dataset.optional = t.optional ? '1' : '0';
        btn.setAttribute('role','tab');
        btn.addEventListener('click',()=>{
          activateSection(section.id);
        });
        btnWrap.appendChild(btn);
      });

      topbar.appendChild(btnWrap);

      // åˆ‡æ¢å¯é€‰ç±»å‹æ˜¾ç¤º/éšè—
      let optionalShown = false;
      const syncOptionalVisibility = () => {
        document.querySelectorAll('[data-optional=\'1\']').forEach(el=>{
          el.classList.toggle('hidden', !optionalShown);
        });
      };
      function handleSearch(){
        const v = (input.value || '').trim();
        if (v === '72875') { optionalShown = true; syncOptionalVisibility(); }
        else if (v === '0') { optionalShown = false; syncOptionalVisibility(); }
      }
      searchBtn.addEventListener('click', handleSearch);
      input.addEventListener('keydown', (e)=>{ if (e.key === 'Enter') handleSearch(); });
      // åˆå§‹åŒ–ä¸€æ¬¡
      syncOptionalVisibility();

      // å†…å®¹æ ‡é¢˜ç‚¹å‡»åŒæ ·å¯æŠ˜å /å±•å¼€å¹¶å®šä½
      content.addEventListener('click', (e)=>{
        const h = e.target.closest('.type-title');
        if (!h) return;
        const targetId = h.dataset.target;
        if (targetId) activateSection(targetId);
      });

      // é»˜è®¤ä¸æ»šåŠ¨åˆ°ä»»ä½•ç±»å‹ï¼Œä¿æŒåœ¨é¡¶éƒ¨
      document.querySelectorAll('.section').forEach(sec=>sec.classList.add('collapsed'));
    }

    Promise.all(types.map(t=>loadScript(t.file))).then(render).catch(console.error);
  </script>
</body>
</html>

```

```html
      s.src = src; s.onload = res; s.onerror = () => rej(new Error('åŠ è½½å¤±è´¥:'+src));
      document.head.appendChild(s);
    });

    function createCard(item){

      if(item.cover) a.style.backgroundImage=`url('${item.cover}')`;
      const info=document.createElement('div'); info.className='info';

      const text = item.summary || item.description || '';
      const p=document.createElement('p'); p.className='summary'; p.textContent=text;
      const desc=document.createElement('p'); desc.className='desc'; desc.textContent=item.description || '';
      info.appendChild(titleEl); info.appendChild(p); info.appendChild(desc);
      a.appendChild(info); return a;
    }

    function activateSection(sectionId){
      document.querySelectorAll('.type-btn').forEach(b=>{
        b.classList.toggle('active', b.dataset.target === sectionId);
      });
      document.querySelectorAll('.section').forEach(sec=>{
        sec.classList.toggle('collapsed', sec.id !== sectionId);
      });
      const target = document.getElementById(sectionId);
      if (target) {
        const topbar = document.getElementById('topbar');
        const offset = (topbar ? topbar.offsetHeight : 0) + 8; // é€‚å½“ç•™ç™½
        const y = target.getBoundingClientRect().top + window.pageYOffset - offset;
        window.scrollTo({ top: y, behavior: 'smooth' });
      }
    }

    function render(){
      const content=document.getElementById('content');
      const topbar=document.getElementById('topbar');
      const input = document.getElementById('optional-key');
      const searchBtn = document.getElementById('optional-search');

      // é¡¶éƒ¨æŒ‰é’®
      const btnWrap=document.createElement('div'); btnWrap.className='types';
      btnWrap.setAttribute('role','tablist');

      // å›åˆ°é¡¶éƒ¨æŒ‰é’®
      const homeBtn=document.createElement('button');
      homeBtn.className='type-btn';
      homeBtn.textContent='é¦–é¡µ';
      homeBtn.addEventListener('click',()=>{
        // æ¸…é™¤æ¿€æ´»
        document.querySelectorAll('.type-btn').forEach(b=>b.classList.remove('active'));
        // æŠ˜å æ‰€æœ‰ç±»å‹
        document.querySelectorAll('.section').forEach(sec=>sec.classList.add('collapsed'));
        // å¹³æ»‘æ»šåŠ¨åˆ°æ ‡é¢˜ä½ç½®ï¼ˆè€ƒè™‘é¡¶éƒ¨å¯¼èˆªé«˜åº¦åç§»ï¼‰
        const topbar = document.getElementById('topbar');
        const header = document.querySelector('.title-row') || document.querySelector('h1');
        const offset = (topbar ? topbar.offsetHeight : 0) + 8;
        const y = (header ? header.getBoundingClientRect().top + window.pageYOffset : 0) - offset;
        window.scrollTo({ top: y, behavior: 'smooth' });
      });
      btnWrap.appendChild(homeBtn);

      types.forEach((t, idx)=>{
        const store=window.linkStore||{}; const data=store[t.id];
        if(!Array.isArray(data) || !data.length) return;

        // section
        const section=document.createElement('section');
        section.className='section';
        section.id = `section-${t.id}`;
        section.dataset.optional = t.optional ? '1' : '0';
        section.innerHTML=`<h2 class=\"type-title\" data-target=\"section-${t.id}\">${t.name}</h2>`;
        const grid=document.createElement('div'); grid.className='grid';
        data.forEach(item=>grid.appendChild(createCard(item)));
        section.appendChild(grid);
        content.appendChild(section);

        // nav button
        const btn=document.createElement('button');
        btn.className='type-btn';
        btn.textContent=t.name;
        btn.dataset.target = section.id;
        btn.dataset.optional = t.optional ? '1' : '0';
        btn.setAttribute('role','tab');
        btn.addEventListener('click',()=>{
          activateSection(section.id);
        });
        btnWrap.appendChild(btn);
      });

      topbar.appendChild(btnWrap);

      // åˆ‡æ¢å¯é€‰ç±»å‹æ˜¾ç¤º/éšè—
      let optionalShown = false;
      const syncOptionalVisibility = () => {
        document.querySelectorAll('[data-optional=\'1\']').forEach(el=>{
          el.classList.toggle('hidden', !optionalShown);
        });
      };
      function handleSearch(){
        const v = (input.value || '').trim();
        if (v === '72875') { optionalShown = true; syncOptionalVisibility(); }
        else if (v === '0') { optionalShown = false; syncOptionalVisibility(); }
      }
      searchBtn.addEventListener('click', handleSearch);
      input.addEventListener('keydown', (e)=>{ if (e.key === 'Enter') handleSearch(); });
      // åˆå§‹åŒ–ä¸€æ¬¡
      syncOptionalVisibility();

      // å†…å®¹æ ‡é¢˜ç‚¹å‡»åŒæ ·å¯æŠ˜å /å±•å¼€å¹¶å®šä½
      content.addEventListener('click', (e)=>{
        const h = e.target.closest('.type-title');
        if (!h) return;
        const targetId = h.dataset.target;
        if (targetId) activateSection(targetId);
      });

      // é»˜è®¤ä¸æ»šåŠ¨åˆ°ä»»ä½•ç±»å‹ï¼Œä¿æŒåœ¨é¡¶éƒ¨
      document.querySelectorAll('.section').forEach(sec=>sec.classList.add('collapsed'));
    }

    Promise.all(types.map(t=>loadScript(t.file))).then(render).catch(console.error);
  </script>
</body>
</html>

```

- æ–°å¢è®¾è®¡å˜é‡ï¼ˆCSS variablesï¼‰ï¼šç»Ÿä¸€èƒŒæ™¯ã€æ–‡å­—ã€æè¾¹ã€ä¸»è‰²ä¸é˜´å½±ï¼Œä¾¿äºæ•´ä½“è°ƒè‰²ã€‚
- å±…ä¸­å®¹å™¨ `.page`ï¼šé™åˆ¶å®½åº¦ï¼Œæ•´ä½“æ›´ç¨³é‡ï¼Œå·¦å³ç•™ç™½æ›´èˆ’é€‚ã€‚

```html
  <script>
    /*
      å‡è®¾æ¯ä¸ªæ•°æ®æ–‡ä»¶ä¸­å®šä¹‰äº†å¦‚ä¸‹æ ¼å¼çš„æ•°ç»„ï¼š
      const links = [ { title, url, description } ]
    */
  </script>

  <script>
    const loadScript = src => new Promise((res, rej) => {
      const s = document.createElement('script');
      s.src = src; s.onload = res; s.onerror = () => rej(new Error('åŠ è½½å¤±è´¥:'+src));
      document.head.appendChild(s);
    });

    function createCard(item){
      const a=document.createElement('a'); a.className='card'; a.href=item.url; a.target='_blank'; a.rel='noopener noreferrer';
      if(item.cover) a.style.backgroundImage=`url('${item.cover}')`;
      const info=document.createElement('div'); info.className='info';
      const titleEl=document.createElement('h3'); titleEl.className='title'; titleEl.textContent=item.title;
      const text = item.summary || item.description || '';
      const p=document.createElement('p'); p.className='summary'; p.textContent=text;
      const desc=document.createElement('p'); desc.className='desc'; desc.textContent=item.description || '';
      info.appendChild(titleEl); info.appendChild(p); info.appendChild(desc);
      a.appendChild(info); return a;
    }

    function activateSection(sectionId){
      document.querySelectorAll('.type-btn').forEach(b=>{
        b.classList.toggle('active', b.dataset.target === sectionId);
      });
      document.querySelectorAll('.section').forEach(sec=>{
        sec.classList.toggle('collapsed', sec.id !== sectionId);
      });
      const target = document.getElementById(sectionId);
      if (target) {
        const topbar = document.getElementById('topbar');
        const offset = (topbar ? topbar.offsetHeight : 0) + 8; // é€‚å½“ç•™ç™½
        const y = target.getBoundingClientRect().top + window.pageYOffset - offset;
        window.scrollTo({ top: y, behavior: 'smooth' });
      }
    }

    function render(){
      const content=document.getElementById('content');
      const topbar=document.getElementById('topbar');
      const input = document.getElementById('optional-key');
      const searchBtn = document.getElementById('optional-search');

      // é¡¶éƒ¨æŒ‰é’®
      const btnWrap=document.createElement('div'); btnWrap.className='types';
      btnWrap.setAttribute('role','tablist');

      // å›åˆ°é¡¶éƒ¨æŒ‰é’®
      const homeBtn=document.createElement('button');
      homeBtn.className='type-btn';
      homeBtn.textContent='é¦–é¡µ';
      homeBtn.addEventListener('click',()=>{
        // æ¸…é™¤æ¿€æ´»
        document.querySelectorAll('.type-btn').forEach(b=>b.classList.remove('active'));
        // æŠ˜å æ‰€æœ‰ç±»å‹
        document.querySelectorAll('.section').forEach(sec=>sec.classList.add('collapsed'));
        // å¹³æ»‘æ»šåŠ¨åˆ°æ ‡é¢˜ä½ç½®ï¼ˆè€ƒè™‘é¡¶éƒ¨å¯¼èˆªé«˜åº¦åç§»ï¼‰
        const topbar = document.getElementById('topbar');
        const header = document.querySelector('.title-row') || document.querySelector('h1');
        const offset = (topbar ? topbar.offsetHeight : 0) + 8;
        const y = (header ? header.getBoundingClientRect().top + window.pageYOffset : 0) - offset;
        window.scrollTo({ top: y, behavior: 'smooth' });
      });
      btnWrap.appendChild(homeBtn);

      types.forEach((t, idx)=>{
        const store=window.linkStore||{}; const data=store[t.id];
        if(!Array.isArray(data) || !data.length) return;

        // section
        const section=document.createElement('section');
        section.className='section';
        section.id = `section-${t.id}`;
        section.dataset.optional = t.optional ? '1' : '0';
        section.innerHTML=`<h2 class=\"type-title\" data-target=\"section-${t.id}\">${t.name}</h2>`;
        const grid=document.createElement('div'); grid.className='grid';
        data.forEach(item=>grid.appendChild(createCard(item)));
        section.appendChild(grid);
        content.appendChild(section);

        // nav button
        const btn=document.createElement('button');
        btn.className='type-btn';
        btn.textContent=t.name;
        btn.dataset.target = section.id;
        btn.dataset.optional = t.optional ? '1' : '0';
        btn.setAttribute('role','tab');
        btn.addEventListener('click',()=>{
          activateSection(section.id);
        });
        btnWrap.appendChild(btn);
      });

      topbar.appendChild(btnWrap);

      // åˆ‡æ¢å¯é€‰ç±»å‹æ˜¾ç¤º/éšè—
      let optionalShown = false;
      const syncOptionalVisibility = () => {
        document.querySelectorAll('[data-optional=\'1\']').forEach(el=>{
          el.classList.toggle('hidden', !optionalShown);
        });
      };
      function handleSearch(){
        const v = (input.value || '').trim();
        if (v === '72875') { optionalShown = true; syncOptionalVisibility(); }
        else if (v === '0') { optionalShown = false; syncOptionalVisibility(); }
      }
      searchBtn.addEventListener('click', handleSearch);
      input.addEventListener('keydown', (e)=>{ if (e.key === 'Enter') handleSearch(); });
      // åˆå§‹åŒ–ä¸€æ¬¡
      syncOptionalVisibility();

      // å†…å®¹æ ‡é¢˜ç‚¹å‡»åŒæ ·å¯æŠ˜å /å±•å¼€å¹¶å®šä½
      content.addEventListener('click', (e)=>{
        const h = e.target.closest('.type-title');
        if (!h) return;
        const targetId = h.dataset.target;
        if (targetId) activateSection(targetId);
      });

      // é»˜è®¤ä¸æ»šåŠ¨åˆ°ä»»ä½•ç±»å‹ï¼Œä¿æŒåœ¨é¡¶éƒ¨
      document.querySelectorAll('.section').forEach(sec=>sec.classList.add('collapsed'));
    }

    Promise.all(types.map(t=>loadScript(t.file))).then(render).catch(console.error);
  </script>
</body>
</html>
```

å·²æ”¹ä¸ºç™¾åˆ†æ¯”ç•™ç™½å¹¶æ’æ»¿å…¨å®½ï¼š
- åœ¨ `:root` ä¸­æ–°å¢å˜é‡ï¼š
  - `--side-gutter`: æ§åˆ¶å·¦å³ç•™ç™½æ¯”ä¾‹ï¼ˆç™¾åˆ†æ¯”ï¼‰ã€‚ç¤ºä¾‹ï¼š6%ï¼Œå¯æ”¹ 5%/8%/10%...
- ä¿®æ”¹ `.page`ï¼š
  - ç°åœ¨ä½¿ç”¨ `width: 100%` å’Œ `padding: 0 var(--side-gutter) 24px`ï¼Œä»¥ç™¾åˆ†æ¯”ç•™ç™½æ’‘æ»¡å±å¹•ã€‚

ä½ å¯ä»¥åœ¨ `:root` çš„ `--side-gutter` å¤„ç›´æ¥è°ƒæ•´ç™¾åˆ†æ¯”ç•™ç™½ã€‚

---

**User**

å·¦å³ä¸è¦æœ‰ä»»ä½•ç•™ç™½ï¼Œç›´æ¥ç›´æ¥ç››æ»¡æ•´ä¸ªå±å¹•

---

**Cursor**

I'll remove all horizontal padding so the layout spans edge-to-edge, then adjust the nav's inner padding to avoid any left margin. Proceeding to update the styles.

```html
<!DOCTYPE html>
<html lang="zh-CN">
<head>
  <meta charset="UTF-8" />
  <meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1.0" />
  <link rel="icon" type="image/png" href="favicon.png" />
  <title>æˆ‘çš„æ”¶è—å¤¹</title>
  <style>
    :root {
      --bg: #f5f7fb;
      --surface: #ffffff;
      --surface-rgb: 255,255,255;
      --text: #2f3440;
      --muted: #6b7280;
      --border: #e6e8ee;
      --accent: #5b8def;
      --accent-600: #3f73e8;
      --shadow: 0 2px 6px rgba(0,0,0,.08);
      --shadow-lg: 0 10px 24px rgba(0,0,0,.12);
      --radius: 12px;
      /* ç•™ç™½æ¯”ä¾‹(%)ï¼šä¿®æ”¹æ­¤å˜é‡å³å¯æ§åˆ¶å·¦å³ç™¾åˆ†æ¯”ç•™ç™½ï¼Œæ¯”å¦‚ 5% / 8% / 10% */
      --side-gutter: 6%;
    }
    body {font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; margin: 0; padding: 0; background: var(--bg); color: var(--text);}    
    /* é¡µé¢å·¦å³æ— ç•™ç™½ï¼Œé“ºæ»¡å…¨å®½ */
    .page {width: 100%; max-width: none; margin: 0; padding: 0;}
    h1 {text-align:left; font-size:18px; margin-bottom:24px; color: var(--text);}    
    section {margin-bottom: 40px;}
          h2 {border-left: 4px solid var(--accent); padding-left: 8px; color: var(--accent);}
      .type-title {cursor:pointer;}
    ul {list-style:none; padding:0;}
    li {background:#fff; margin:8px 0; padding:12px 16px; border-radius:6px; box-shadow:0 1px 3px rgba(0,0,0,.1);}  
    a {text-decoration:none; color:#333; font-weight:bold;}
    p {margin:4px 0 0; color:#666; font-size:14px;}
    /* ç½‘æ ¼å¡ç‰‡æ ·å¼ */
    .grid {display:grid; grid-template-columns:repeat(auto-fill,minmax(220px,1fr)); gap:16px; margin:16px 0;}
    .card {position:relative; display:block; height:160px; border-radius: var(--radius); overflow:hidden; background-size:cover; background-position:center; box-shadow: var(--shadow); transition:box-shadow .2s; color:#fff; text-decoration:none;}
    /* 1) æ‚¬åœæ—¶å¡ç‰‡ä¸ç§»åŠ¨ï¼Œä»…å¾®è°ƒé˜´å½±ï¼ˆå¦‚ä¸éœ€è¦å¯åˆ é™¤ä¸‹ä¸€è¡Œï¼‰ */
    .card:hover {transform:none; box-shadow:0 4px 12px rgba(0,0,0,.18);} 
    /* 2) å»é™¤æ•´å¡åŠé€é®ç½©ï¼Œæ”¹ä¸ºåº•éƒ¨æ¸å˜ä¿¡æ¯æ  */
    /* 2) åº•éƒ¨æ¸å˜ä¿¡æ¯æ ï¼šä¸Šç¼“ä¸‹æ€¥ï¼ˆå¤šæ®µè‰²æ ‡æ¨¡æ‹Ÿéçº¿æ€§è¿‡æ¸¡ï¼‰ */
    .info {position:absolute; left:0; right:0; bottom:0; padding:10px; background:linear-gradient(to top,
      rgba(0,0,0,.75) 0%,
      rgba(0,0,0,.60) 35%,
      rgba(0,0,0,.30) 70%,
      rgba(0,0,0,0) 100%
    ); transition: top .25s ease, padding .25s ease;}
    /* æ‚¬åœæ—¶ï¼Œä¿¡æ¯æ æ‰©å±•åˆ°æ•´å¼ å¡ç‰‡ */
    .card:hover .info {top:0;}
    /* å åŠ ä¸€ä¸ªå¯åŠ¨ç”»çš„åŠé€æ˜èƒŒæ™¯å±‚ */
    .info::before {content:""; position:absolute; inset:0; background:rgba(0,0,0,.6); opacity:0; transition:opacity .25s ease;}
    .card:hover .info::before {opacity:1;}
    /* æ–‡æœ¬ç½®äºåŠé€æ˜å±‚ä¹‹ä¸Š */
    .info > * {position:relative; z-index:1;}
    /* 5) æ ‡æ³¨: å¯åœ¨æ­¤è°ƒæ•´æ ‡é¢˜é¢œè‰²ä¸è¡Œè· */
    .info .title {margin:0; font-size:16px; line-height:1.2; color:#ffffff;}
    /* 4) summary æ˜¾ç¤ºä¸¤è¡Œï¼Œå¹¶å¯åœ¨æ­¤è°ƒæ•´é¢œè‰²ä¸è¡Œè· */
    .info .summary {margin:4px 0 0; font-size:12px; line-height:1.4; color:rgba(255,255,255,.9);
      /* è®©å†…å®¹å…ˆè‡ªç„¶æ¢è¡Œåˆ°ç¬¬äºŒè¡Œï¼Œè¶…å‡ºç¬¬äºŒè¡Œå†çœç•¥ */
      white-space: normal; word-break: break-word; overflow: hidden;
      display: -webkit-box; -webkit-box-orient: vertical; -webkit-line-clamp: 2; line-clamp: 2;
    }
    /* hover æ—¶æ˜¾ç¤ºæ›´è¯¦ç»†æè¿°ï¼Œéšè— summary */
    .info .desc {display:none; margin:6px 0 0; font-size:12px; line-height:1.5; color:rgba(255,255,255,.95);} /* å¯è°ƒé¢œè‰²ä¸è¡Œè· */
    .card:hover .info .desc {display:block;}
    .card:hover .info .summary {display:none;}
    /* é¡¶éƒ¨ç±»å‹å¯¼èˆªä¸æŠ˜å æ ·å¼ */
    .topbar {position:sticky; top:0; z-index:10; background: rgba(var(--surface-rgb), .9); padding:8px 0; margin:0 0 12px; box-shadow:0 1px 4px rgba(0,0,0,.06); backdrop-filter: saturate(140%) blur(8px);} 
    .topbar .types {display:flex; gap:8px; flex-wrap:wrap; justify-content:flex-start; padding-left:0;}
    .type-btn {border:1px solid var(--border); background: var(--surface); color: var(--text); padding:6px 12px; border-radius:999px; cursor:pointer; font-size:13px; transition:background .2s, color .2s, border-color .2s, box-shadow .2s;}
    .type-btn:hover {background:#f3f6ff; border-color:#d5def8;}
    .type-btn.active {background: var(--accent); border-color: var(--accent); color:#fff; box-shadow: 0 4px 12px rgba(91,141,239,.3);}    
    .section.collapsed .grid {display:none;}
    .hidden {display:none !important;}

    /* æ ‡é¢˜è¡Œä¸éšè”½æŒ‰é’®æ ·å¼ */
    .title-row {display:flex; align-items:center; gap:8px; padding-top: 10px;}
    .title-row h1 {flex:1 1 auto;}
    .action-right {flex:0 0 auto; display:flex; align-items:center; gap:6px;}
    .search-input {height:30px; padding:0 10px; border:1px solid var(--border); border-radius:16px; font-size:12px; width:160px; background: var(--surface); color: var(--text); transition:border-color .2s, box-shadow .2s;}
    .search-input:focus {outline:none; border-color:#c7d2fe; box-shadow:0 0 0 3px rgba(91,141,239,.18);}    
    .type-btn.ghost {background:transparent; border-color:var(--border); color:var(--muted); padding:6px 10px; font-size:12px; border-radius:999px;}
    .type-btn.ghost:hover {background:#f6f8ff; color:#55617c;}
  </style>
</head>
<body>
  <div class="page">
    <div class="title-row">
      <h1>æˆ‘çš„ç½‘ç«™æ”¶è—</h1>
      <div class="action-right">
        <input id="optional-key" class="search-input" placeholder="è¾“å…¥" />
        <button id="optional-search" class="type-btn ghost" title="æœç´¢">æœç´¢</button>
      </div>
    </div>
    <nav id="topbar" class="topbar"></nav>
    <!-- å†…å®¹å®¹å™¨ -->
    <div id="content"></div>
  </div>

  <!-- å¼•å…¥ç±»å‹æ˜ å°„ -->
  <script src="js/type.js"></script>

  <script>
    /*
      å‡è®¾æ¯ä¸ªæ•°æ®æ–‡ä»¶ä¸­å®šä¹‰äº†å¦‚ä¸‹æ ¼å¼çš„æ•°ç»„ï¼š
      const links = [ { title, url, description } ]
    */
  </script>

  <script>
    const loadScript = src => new Promise((res, rej) => {
      const s = document.createElement('script');
      s.src = src; s.onload = res; s.onerror = () => rej(new Error('åŠ è½½å¤±è´¥:'+src));
      document.head.appendChild(s);
    });

    function createCard(item){
      const a=document.createElement('a'); a.className='card'; a.href=item.url; a.target='_blank'; a.rel='noopener noreferrer';
      if(item.cover) a.style.backgroundImage=`url('${item.cover}')`;
      const info=document.createElement('div'); info.className='info';
      const titleEl=document.createElement('h3'); titleEl.className='title'; titleEl.textContent=item.title;
      const text = item.summary || item.description || '';
      const p=document.createElement('p'); p.className='summary'; p.textContent=text;
      const desc=document.createElement('p'); desc.className='desc'; desc.textContent=item.description || '';
      info.appendChild(titleEl); info.appendChild(p); info.appendChild(desc);
      a.appendChild(info); return a;
    }

    function activateSection(sectionId){
      document.querySelectorAll('.type-btn').forEach(b=>{
        b.classList.toggle('active', b.dataset.target === sectionId);
      });
      document.querySelectorAll('.section').forEach(sec=>{
        sec.classList.toggle('collapsed', sec.id !== sectionId);
      });
      const target = document.getElementById(sectionId);
      if (target) {
        const topbar = document.getElementById('topbar');
        const offset = (topbar ? topbar.offsetHeight : 0) + 8; // é€‚å½“ç•™ç™½
        const y = target.getBoundingClientRect().top + window.pageYOffset - offset;
        window.scrollTo({ top: y, behavior: 'smooth' });
      }
    }

    function render(){
      const content=document.getElementById('content');
      const topbar=document.getElementById('topbar');
      const input = document.getElementById('optional-key');
      const searchBtn = document.getElementById('optional-search');

      // é¡¶éƒ¨æŒ‰é’®
      const btnWrap=document.createElement('div'); btnWrap.className='types';
      btnWrap.setAttribute('role','tablist');

      // å›åˆ°é¡¶éƒ¨æŒ‰é’®
      const homeBtn=document.createElement('button');
      homeBtn.className='type-btn';
      homeBtn.textContent='é¦–é¡µ';
      homeBtn.addEventListener('click',()=>{
        // æ¸…é™¤æ¿€æ´»
        document.querySelectorAll('.type-btn').forEach(b=>b.classList.remove('active'));
        // æŠ˜å æ‰€æœ‰ç±»å‹
        document.querySelectorAll('.section').forEach(sec=>sec.classList.add('collapsed'));
        // å¹³æ»‘æ»šåŠ¨åˆ°æ ‡é¢˜ä½ç½®ï¼ˆè€ƒè™‘é¡¶éƒ¨å¯¼èˆªé«˜åº¦åç§»ï¼‰
        const topbar = document.getElementById('topbar');
        const header = document.querySelector('.title-row') || document.querySelector('h1');
        const offset = (topbar ? topbar.offsetHeight : 0) + 8;
        const y = (header ? header.getBoundingClientRect().top + window.pageYOffset : 0) - offset;
        window.scrollTo({ top: y, behavior: 'smooth' });
      });
      btnWrap.appendChild(homeBtn);

      types.forEach((t, idx)=>{
        const store=window.linkStore||{}; const data=store[t.id];
        if(!Array.isArray(data) || !data.length) return;

        // section
        const section=document.createElement('section');
        section.className='section';
        section.id = `section-${t.id}`;
        section.dataset.optional = t.optional ? '1' : '0';
        section.innerHTML=`<h2 class=\"type-title\" data-target=\"section-${t.id}\">${t.name}</h2>`;
        const grid=document.createElement('div'); grid.className='grid';
        data.forEach(item=>grid.appendChild(createCard(item)));
        section.appendChild(grid);
        content.appendChild(section);

        // nav button
        const btn=document.createElement('button');
        btn.className='type-btn';
        btn.textContent=t.name;
        btn.dataset.target = section.id;
        btn.dataset.optional = t.optional ? '1' : '0';
        btn.setAttribute('role','tab');
        btn.addEventListener('click',()=>{
          activateSection(section.id);
        });
        btnWrap.appendChild(btn);
      });

      topbar.appendChild(btnWrap);

      // åˆ‡æ¢å¯é€‰ç±»å‹æ˜¾ç¤º/éšè—
      let optionalShown = false;
      const syncOptionalVisibility = () => {
        document.querySelectorAll('[data-optional=\'1\']').forEach(el=>{
          el.classList.toggle('hidden', !optionalShown);
        });
      };
      function handleSearch(){
        const v = (input.value || '').trim();
        if (v === '72875') { optionalShown = true; syncOptionalVisibility(); }
        else if (v === '0') { optionalShown = false; syncOptionalVisibility(); }
      }
      searchBtn.addEventListener('click', handleSearch);
      input.addEventListener('keydown', (e)=>{ if (e.key === 'Enter') handleSearch(); });
      // åˆå§‹åŒ–ä¸€æ¬¡
      syncOptionalVisibility();

      // å†…å®¹æ ‡é¢˜ç‚¹å‡»åŒæ ·å¯æŠ˜å /å±•å¼€å¹¶å®šä½
      content.addEventListener('click', (e)=>{
        const h = e.target.closest('.type-title');
        if (!h) return;
        const targetId = h.dataset.target;
        if (targetId) activateSection(targetId);
      });

      // é»˜è®¤ä¸æ»šåŠ¨åˆ°ä»»ä½•ç±»å‹ï¼Œä¿æŒåœ¨é¡¶éƒ¨
      document.querySelectorAll('.section').forEach(sec=>sec.classList.add('collapsed'));
    }

    Promise.all(types.map(t=>loadScript(t.file))).then(render).catch(console.error);
  </script>
</body>
</html>

```

å·²ç§»é™¤å·¦å³ç•™ç™½ï¼š
- `.page` å»æ‰æ‰€æœ‰æ°´å¹³ padding ä¸ marginï¼Œé“ºæ»¡å…¨å®½ã€‚
- `.topbar .types` å»æ‰å·¦ä¾§å†…è¾¹è·ï¼Œå¯¼èˆªç´§è´´å·¦è¾¹ç¼˜ã€‚

éœ€è¦å†ç»™æŸåŒºåŸŸåŠ å†…è¾¹è·æ—¶ï¼Œå¯ä»…åœ¨è¯¥å±€éƒ¨å¢åŠ ï¼Œä¸å½±å“å…¨å±€é“ºæ»¡ã€‚

---

**User**

1. å·¦å³è¿˜æ˜¯åŠ ä¸Šä¸€ç‚¹ç•™ç™½å§ï¼Œ è¿˜æ˜¯ä¿æŒç™¾åˆ†æ¯”å¯ä»¥è°ƒæ•´ï¼Œ å¹¶ä¸”ä¿æŒå†…å®¹å®Œå…¨å±…ä¸­ 2. å°†å­—ä½“æ›¿æ¢ä¸ºæˆ‘æ–°åŠ å…¥çš„SmileySans-Oblique.ttf

---

**Cursor**

I'll adjust the layout to reintroduce adjustable percentage side gutters centered via the `.page` wrapper, and load your `SmileySans-Oblique.ttf` using `@font-face`, applying it site-wide. I'll update `index.html` styles accordingly.

```html
      if(item.cover) a.style.backgroundImage=`url('${item.cover}')`;

      const p=document.createElement('p'); p.className='summary'; p.textContent=text;
      const desc=document.createElement('p'); desc.className='desc'; desc.textContent=item.description || '';
      info.appendChild(titleEl); info.appendChild(p); info.appendChild(desc);
      a.appendChild(info); return a;
    }

    function activateSection(sectionId){
      document.querySelectorAll('.type-btn').forEach(b=>{
        b.classList.toggle('active', b.dataset.target === sectionId);
      });
      document.querySelectorAll('.section').forEach(sec=>{
        sec.classList.toggle('collapsed', sec.id !== sectionId);
      });
      const target = document.getElementById(sectionId);
      if (target) {
        const topbar = document.getElementById('topbar');
        const offset = (topbar ? topbar.offsetHeight : 0) + 8; // é€‚å½“ç•™ç™½
        const y = target.getBoundingClientRect().top + window.pageYOffset - offset;
        window.scrollTo({ top: y, behavior: 'smooth' });
      }
    }

    function render(){
      const content=document.getElementById('content');
      const topbar=document.getElementById('topbar');
      const input = document.getElementById('optional-key');
      const searchBtn = document.getElementById('optional-search');

      // é¡¶éƒ¨æŒ‰é’®
      const btnWrap=document.createElement('div'); btnWrap.className='types';
      btnWrap.setAttribute('role','tablist');

      // å›åˆ°é¡¶éƒ¨æŒ‰é’®
      const homeBtn=document.createElement('button');
      homeBtn.className='type-btn';
      homeBtn.textContent='é¦–é¡µ';
      homeBtn.addEventListener('click',()=>{
        // æ¸…é™¤æ¿€æ´»
        document.querySelectorAll('.type-btn').forEach(b=>b.classList.remove('active'));
        // æŠ˜å æ‰€æœ‰ç±»å‹
        document.querySelectorAll('.section').forEach(sec=>sec.classList.add('collapsed'));
        // å¹³æ»‘æ»šåŠ¨åˆ°æ ‡é¢˜ä½ç½®ï¼ˆè€ƒè™‘é¡¶éƒ¨å¯¼èˆªé«˜åº¦åç§»ï¼‰
        const topbar = document.getElementById('topbar');
        const header = document.querySelector('.title-row') || document.querySelector('h1');
        const offset = (topbar ? topbar.offsetHeight : 0) + 8;
        const y = (header ? header.getBoundingClientRect().top + window.pageYOffset : 0) - offset;
        window.scrollTo({ top: y, behavior: 'smooth' });
      });
      btnWrap.appendChild(homeBtn);

      types.forEach((t, idx)=>{
        const store=window.linkStore||{}; const data=store[t.id];
        if(!Array.isArray(data) || !data.length) return;

        // section
        const section=document.createElement('section');
        section.className='section';
        section.id = `section-${t.id}`;
        section.dataset.optional = t.optional ? '1' : '0';
        section.innerHTML=`<h2 class=\"type-title\" data-target=\"section-${t.id}\">${t.name}</h2>`;
        const grid=document.createElement('div'); grid.className='grid';
        data.forEach(item=>grid.appendChild(createCard(item)));
        section.appendChild(grid);
        content.appendChild(section);

        // nav button
        const btn=document.createElement('button');
        btn.className='type-btn';
        btn.textContent=t.name;
        btn.dataset.target = section.id;
        btn.dataset.optional = t.optional ? '1' : '0';
        btn.setAttribute('role','tab');
        btn.addEventListener('click',()=>{
          activateSection(section.id);
        });
        btnWrap.appendChild(btn);
      });

      topbar.appendChild(btnWrap);

      // åˆ‡æ¢å¯é€‰ç±»å‹æ˜¾ç¤º/éšè—
      let optionalShown = false;
      const syncOptionalVisibility = () => {
        document.querySelectorAll('[data-optional=\'1\']').forEach(el=>{
          el.classList.toggle('hidden', !optionalShown);
        });
      };
      function handleSearch(){
        const v = (input.value || '').trim();
        if (v === '72875') { optionalShown = true; syncOptionalVisibility(); }
        else if (v === '0') { optionalShown = false; syncOptionalVisibility(); }
      }
      searchBtn.addEventListener('click', handleSearch);
      input.addEventListener('keydown', (e)=>{ if (e.key === 'Enter') handleSearch(); });
      // åˆå§‹åŒ–ä¸€æ¬¡
      syncOptionalVisibility();

      // å†…å®¹æ ‡é¢˜ç‚¹å‡»åŒæ ·å¯æŠ˜å /å±•å¼€å¹¶å®šä½
      content.addEventListener('click', (e)=>{
        const h = e.target.closest('.type-title');
        if (!h) return;
        const targetId = h.dataset.target;
        if (targetId) activateSection(targetId);
      });

      // é»˜è®¤ä¸æ»šåŠ¨åˆ°ä»»ä½•ç±»å‹ï¼Œä¿æŒåœ¨é¡¶éƒ¨
      document.querySelectorAll('.section').forEach(sec=>sec.classList.add('collapsed'));
    }

    Promise.all(types.map(t=>loadScript(t.file))).then(render).catch(console.error);
  </script>
</body>
</html>

```

å·²è°ƒæ•´ï¼š
- æ¢å¤å¯è°ƒç™¾åˆ†æ¯”ç•™ç™½å¹¶ä¿æŒå†…å®¹å±…ä¸­ï¼šåœ¨ `:root` ä¸­ä½¿ç”¨ `--side-gutter`ï¼Œ`.page` ä½¿ç”¨ `padding: 0 var(--side-gutter)`ã€‚ä½ å¯åœ¨ `:root --side-gutter` ä¸­ç›´æ¥æ”¹æˆ 5%/8%/10% ç­‰ã€‚
- æ›¿æ¢å­—ä½“ï¼šé€šè¿‡ `@font-face` å¼•å…¥ `SmileySans-Oblique.ttf` å¹¶åœ¨ `body` ä¸Šåº”ç”¨ã€‚è¯·ç¡®ä¿å­—ä½“æ–‡ä»¶æ”¾åœ¨é¡¹ç›®æ ¹ç›®å½•ï¼Œæ–‡ä»¶åä¸å¤§å°å†™ä¸€è‡´ã€‚

---

**User**

1. ä¸ºä»€ä¹ˆç•™ç™½äº†ä¹‹åï¼Œä¼šæœ‰ä¸€ä¸ªæ¨ªå‘çš„æ»šåŠ¨æ¡ï¼Œå¹¶ä¸”å³è¾¹è¢«è£å‰ªæ‰äº†ä¸€éƒ¨åˆ†ï¼Œ æˆ‘æƒ³æ‰€æœ‰çš„å†…å®¹åœ¨ä¸€å±æ˜¾ç¤ºå¾—ä¸‹å¹¶ä¸”ä¸éœ€è¦æ»šåŠ¨æ¡ 2. å°†å¡ç‰‡ä¸Šçš„summarå’Œè¯¦ç»†æè¿°æ¢æˆé»˜è®¤å­—ä½“

---

**Cursor**

I'll fix the horizontal scroll by making the container use border-box sizing (so percentage side paddings don't exceed 100% width) and also set summary/desc to a default font. Now updating index.html styles.

```html

      --bg: #f5f7fb;

      --radius: 12px;
      /* ç•™ç™½æ¯”ä¾‹(%)ï¼šä¿®æ”¹æ­¤å˜é‡å³å¯æ§åˆ¶å·¦å³ç™¾åˆ†æ¯”ç•™ç™½ï¼Œæ¯”å¦‚ 5% / 8% / 10% */
      --side-gutter: 6%;
    }
    /* è®©æ‰€æœ‰å…ƒç´ é‡‡ç”¨ border-boxï¼Œé¿å…ç™¾åˆ†æ¯” padding é€ æˆæ¨ªå‘æº¢å‡º */
    *, *::before, *::after { box-sizing: border-box; }
    /* å¼•å…¥ SmileySans-Oblique.ttf å­—ä½“ï¼ˆæ”¾åœ¨ç«™ç‚¹æ ¹ç›®å½•ï¼‰ */
    @font-face {
      font-family: 'SmileySans Oblique';
      src: url('SmileySans-Oblique.ttf') format('truetype');
      font-weight: 400;
      font-style: oblique;
      font-display: swap;
    }
    body {font-family: 'SmileySans Oblique', Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; margin: 0; padding: 0; background: var(--bg); color: var(--text);}    
    /* é¡µé¢å·¦å³ç•™ç™½ä½¿ç”¨ç™¾åˆ†æ¯”ï¼ˆ--side-gutterï¼‰ï¼Œå†…å®¹å§‹ç»ˆå±…ä¸­ */
    /* åœ¨æ­¤è°ƒæ•´ç™¾åˆ†æ¯”ç•™ç™½å˜é‡ï¼š:root --side-gutter */
    .page {width: 100%; max-width: none; margin: 0 auto; padding: 0 var(--side-gutter); box-sizing: border-box;}

          h2 {border-left: 4px solid var(--accent); padding-left: 8px; color: var(--accent);}
      .type-title {cursor:pointer;}
    ul {list-style:none; padding:0;}

    /* ç½‘æ ¼å¡ç‰‡æ ·å¼ */
    .grid {display:grid; grid-template-columns:repeat(auto-fill,minmax(220px,1fr)); gap:16px; margin:16px 0;}
    .card {position:relative; display:block; height:160px; border-radius: var(--radius); overflow:hidden; background-size:cover; background-position:center; box-shadow: var(--shadow); transition:box-shadow .2s; color:#fff; text-decoration:none;}
    /* 1) æ‚¬åœæ—¶å¡ç‰‡ä¸ç§»åŠ¨ï¼Œä»…å¾®è°ƒé˜´å½±ï¼ˆå¦‚ä¸éœ€è¦å¯åˆ é™¤ä¸‹ä¸€è¡Œï¼‰ */
    .card:hover {transform:none; box-shadow:0 4px 12px rgba(0,0,0,.18);} 
    /* 2) å»é™¤æ•´å¡åŠé€é®ç½©ï¼Œæ”¹ä¸ºåº•éƒ¨æ¸å˜ä¿¡æ¯æ  */
    /* 2) åº•éƒ¨æ¸å˜ä¿¡æ¯æ ï¼šä¸Šç¼“ä¸‹æ€¥ï¼ˆå¤šæ®µè‰²æ ‡æ¨¡æ‹Ÿéçº¿æ€§è¿‡æ¸¡ï¼‰ */
    .info {position:absolute; left:0; right:0; bottom:0; padding:10px; background:linear-gradient(to top,
      rgba(0,0,0,.75) 0%,

      rgba(0,0,0,0) 100%
    ); transition: top .25s ease, padding .25s ease;}
    /* æ‚¬åœæ—¶ï¼Œä¿¡æ¯æ æ‰©å±•åˆ°æ•´å¼ å¡ç‰‡ */
    .card:hover .info {top:0;}
    /* å åŠ ä¸€ä¸ªå¯åŠ¨ç”»çš„åŠé€æ˜èƒŒæ™¯å±‚ */
    .info::before {content:""; position:absolute; inset:0; background:rgba(0,0,0,.6); opacity:0; transition:opacity .25s ease;}
    .card:hover .info::before {opacity:1;}
    /* æ–‡æœ¬ç½®äºåŠé€æ˜å±‚ä¹‹ä¸Š */
    .info > * {position:relative; z-index:1;}
    /* 5) æ ‡æ³¨: å¯åœ¨æ­¤è°ƒæ•´æ ‡é¢˜é¢œè‰²ä¸è¡Œè· */
    .info .title {margin:0; font-size:16px; line-height:1.2; color:#ffffff;}
    /* 4) summary æ˜¾ç¤ºä¸¤è¡Œï¼Œå¹¶å¯åœ¨æ­¤è°ƒæ•´é¢œè‰²ä¸è¡Œè· */
    .info .summary {margin:4px 0 0; font-size:12px; line-height:1.4; color:rgba(255,255,255,.9);
      /* è®©å†…å®¹å…ˆè‡ªç„¶æ¢è¡Œåˆ°ç¬¬äºŒè¡Œï¼Œè¶…å‡ºç¬¬äºŒè¡Œå†çœç•¥ */
      white-space: normal; word-break: break-word; overflow: hidden;
      display: -webkit-box; -webkit-box-orient: vertical; -webkit-line-clamp: 2; line-clamp: 2;
    }
    /* hover æ—¶æ˜¾ç¤ºæ›´è¯¦ç»†æè¿°ï¼Œéšè— summary */
    .info .desc {display:none; margin:6px 0 0; font-size:12px; line-height:1.5; color:rgba(255,255,255,.95);} /* å¯è°ƒé¢œè‰²ä¸è¡Œè· */
    .card:hover .info .desc {display:block;}
    .card:hover .info .summary {display:none;}
    /* é¡¶éƒ¨ç±»å‹å¯¼èˆªä¸æŠ˜å æ ·å¼ */
    .topbar {position:sticky; top:0; z-index:10; background: rgba(var(--surface-rgb), .9); padding:8px 0; margin:0 0 12px; box-shadow:0 1px 4px rgba(0,0,0,.06); backdrop-filter: saturate(140%) blur(8px);} 
    .topbar .types {display:flex; gap:8px; flex-wrap:wrap; justify-content:flex-start; padding-left:0;}
    .type-btn {border:1px solid var(--border); background: var(--surface); color: var(--text); padding:6px 12px; border-radius:999px; cursor:pointer; font-size:13px; transition:background .2s, color .2s, border-color .2s, box-shadow .2s;}
    .type-btn:hover {background:#f3f6ff; border-color:#d5def8;}
    .type-btn.active {background: var(--accent); border-color: var(--accent); color:#fff; box-shadow: 0 4px 12px rgba(91,141,239,.3);}    
    .section.collapsed .grid {display:none;}
    .hidden {display:none !important;}

    /* æ ‡é¢˜è¡Œä¸éšè”½æŒ‰é’®æ ·å¼ */
    .title-row {display:flex; align-items:center; gap:8px; padding-top: 10px;}
    .title-row h1 {flex:1 1 auto;}
    .action-right {flex:0 0 auto; display:flex; align-items:center; gap:6px;}
    .search-input {height:30px; padding:0 10px; border:1px solid var(--border); border-radius:16px; font-size:12px; width:160px; background: var(--surface); color: var(--text); transition:border-color .2s, box-shadow .2s;}
    .search-input:focus {outline:none; border-color:#c7d2fe; box-shadow:0 0 0 3px rgba(91,141,239,.18);}    
    .type-btn.ghost {background:transparent; border-color:var(--border); color:var(--muted); padding:6px 10px; font-size:12px; border-radius:999px;}
    .type-btn.ghost:hover {background:#f6f8ff; color:#55617c;}

<body>
  <div class="page">
    <div class="title-row">
      <h1>æˆ‘çš„ç½‘ç«™æ”¶è—</h1>
      <div class="action-right">
        <input id="optional-key" class="search-input" placeholder="è¾“å…¥" />
        <button id="optional-search" class="type-btn ghost" title="æœç´¢">æœç´¢</button>
      </div>
    </div>
    <nav id="topbar" class="topbar"></nav>
    <!-- å†…å®¹å®¹å™¨ -->
    <div id="content"></div>
  </div>

  <!-- å¼•å…¥ç±»å‹æ˜ å°„ -->
  <script src="js/type.js"></script>

  <script>
    /*
      å‡è®¾æ¯ä¸ªæ•°æ®æ–‡ä»¶ä¸­å®šä¹‰äº†å¦‚ä¸‹æ ¼å¼çš„æ•°ç»„ï¼š
      const links = [ { title, url, description } ]
    */
  </script>

  <script>
    const loadScript = src => new Promise((res, rej) => {
      const s = document.createElement('script');
      s.src = src; s.onload = res; s.onerror = () => rej(new Error('åŠ è½½å¤±è´¥:'+src));
      document.head.appendChild(s);
    });

    function createCard(item){
      const a=document.createElement('a'); a.className='card'; a.href=item.url; a.target='_blank'; a.rel='noopener noreferrer';
      if(item.cover) a.style.backgroundImage=`url('${item.cover}')`;
      const info=document.createElement('div'); info.className='info';
      const titleEl=document.createElement('h3'); titleEl.className='title'; titleEl.textContent=item.title;
      const text = item.summary || item.description || '';
      const p=document.createElement('p'); p.className='summary'; p.textContent=text;
      const desc=document.createElement('p'); desc.className='desc'; desc.textContent=item.description || '';
      info.appendChild(titleEl); info.appendChild(p); info.appendChild(desc);
      a.appendChild(info); return a;
    }

    function activateSection(sectionId){
      document.querySelectorAll('.type-btn').forEach(b=>{
        b.classList.toggle('active', b.dataset.target === sectionId);
      });
      document.querySelectorAll('.section').forEach(sec=>{
        sec.classList.toggle('collapsed', sec.id !== sectionId);
      });
      const target = document.getElementById(sectionId);
      if (target) {
        const topbar = document.getElementById('topbar');
        const offset = (topbar ? topbar.offsetHeight : 0) + 8; // é€‚å½“ç•™ç™½
        const y = target.getBoundingClientRect().top + window.pageYOffset - offset;
        window.scrollTo({ top: y, behavior: 'smooth' });
      }
    }

    function render(){
      const content=document.getElementById('content');
      const topbar=document.getElementById('topbar');
      const input = document.getElementById('optional-key');
      const searchBtn = document.getElementById('optional-search');

      // é¡¶éƒ¨æŒ‰é’®
      const btnWrap=document.createElement('div'); btnWrap.className='types';
      btnWrap.setAttribute('role','tablist');

      // å›åˆ°é¡¶éƒ¨æŒ‰é’®
      const homeBtn=document.createElement('button');
      homeBtn.className='type-btn';
      homeBtn.textContent='é¦–é¡µ';
      homeBtn.addEventListener('click',()=>{
        // æ¸…é™¤æ¿€æ´»
        document.querySelectorAll('.type-btn').forEach(b=>b.classList.remove('active'));
        // æŠ˜å æ‰€æœ‰ç±»å‹
        document.querySelectorAll('.section').forEach(sec=>sec.classList.add('collapsed'));
        // å¹³æ»‘æ»šåŠ¨åˆ°æ ‡é¢˜ä½ç½®ï¼ˆè€ƒè™‘é¡¶éƒ¨å¯¼èˆªé«˜åº¦åç§»ï¼‰
        const topbar = document.getElementById('topbar');
        const header = document.querySelector('.title-row') || document.querySelector('h1');
        const offset = (topbar ? topbar.offsetHeight : 0) + 8;
        const y = (header ? header.getBoundingClientRect().top + window.pageYOffset : 0) - offset;
        window.scrollTo({ top: y, behavior: 'smooth' });
      });
      btnWrap.appendChild(homeBtn);

      types.forEach((t, idx)=>{
        const store=window.linkStore||{}; const data=store[t.id];
        if(!Array.isArray(data) || !data.length) return;

        // section
        const section=document.createElement('section');
        section.className='section';
        section.id = `section-${t.id}`;
        section.dataset.optional = t.optional ? '1' : '0';
        section.innerHTML=`<h2 class=\"type-title\" data-target=\"section-${t.id}\">${t.name}</h2>`;
        const grid=document.createElement('div'); grid.className='grid';
        data.forEach(item=>grid.appendChild(createCard(item)));
        section.appendChild(grid);
        content.appendChild(section);

        // nav button
        const btn=document.createElement('button');
        btn.className='type-btn';
        btn.textContent=t.name;
        btn.dataset.target = section.id;
        btn.dataset.optional = t.optional ? '1' : '0';
        btn.setAttribute('role','tab');
        btn.addEventListener('click',()=>{
          activateSection(section.id);
        });
        btnWrap.appendChild(btn);
      });

      topbar.appendChild(btnWrap);

      // åˆ‡æ¢å¯é€‰ç±»å‹æ˜¾ç¤º/éšè—
      let optionalShown = false;
      const syncOptionalVisibility = () => {
        document.querySelectorAll('[data-optional=\'1\']').forEach(el=>{
          el.classList.toggle('hidden', !optionalShown);
        });
      };
      function handleSearch(){
        const v = (input.value || '').trim();
        if (v === '72875') { optionalShown = true; syncOptionalVisibility(); }
        else if (v === '0') { optionalShown = false; syncOptionalVisibility(); }
      }
      searchBtn.addEventListener('click', handleSearch);
      input.addEventListener('keydown', (e)=>{ if (e.key === 'Enter') handleSearch(); });
      // åˆå§‹åŒ–ä¸€æ¬¡
      syncOptionalVisibility();

      // å†…å®¹æ ‡é¢˜ç‚¹å‡»åŒæ ·å¯æŠ˜å /å±•å¼€å¹¶å®šä½
      content.addEventListener('click', (e)=>{
        const h = e.target.closest('.type-title');
        if (!h) return;
        const targetId = h.dataset.target;
        if (targetId) activateSection(targetId);
      });

      // é»˜è®¤ä¸æ»šåŠ¨åˆ°ä»»ä½•ç±»å‹ï¼Œä¿æŒåœ¨é¡¶éƒ¨
      document.querySelectorAll('.section').forEach(sec=>sec.classList.add('collapsed'));
    }

    Promise.all(types.map(t=>loadScript(t.file))).then(render).catch(console.error);
  </script>
</body>
</html>

```

```html

    *, *::before, *::after { box-sizing: border-box; }

    @font-face {

      font-weight: 400;

      font-display: swap;
    }
    body {font-family: 'SmileySans Oblique', Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; margin: 0; padding: 0; background: var(--bg); color: var(--text);}

    /* åœ¨æ­¤è°ƒæ•´ç™¾åˆ†æ¯”ç•™ç™½å˜é‡ï¼š:root --side-gutter */
    .page {width: 100%; max-width: none; margin: 0 auto; padding: 0 var(--side-gutter); box-sizing: border-box;}

          h2 {border-left: 4px solid var(--accent); padding-left: 8px; color: var(--accent);}
      .type-title {cursor:pointer;}

    a {text-decoration:none; color:#333; font-weight:bold;}
    p {margin:4px 0 0; color:#666; font-size:14px;}
    /* ç½‘æ ¼å¡ç‰‡æ ·å¼ */
    .grid {display:grid; grid-template-columns:repeat(auto-fill,minmax(220px,1fr)); gap:16px; margin:16px 0;}
    .card {position:relative; display:block; height:160px; border-radius: var(--radius); overflow:hidden; background-size:cover; background-position:center; box-shadow: var(--shadow); transition:box-shadow .2s; color:#fff; text-decoration:none;}
    /* 1) æ‚¬åœæ—¶å¡ç‰‡ä¸ç§»åŠ¨ï¼Œä»…å¾®è°ƒé˜´å½±ï¼ˆå¦‚ä¸éœ€è¦å¯åˆ é™¤ä¸‹ä¸€è¡Œï¼‰ */
    .card:hover {transform:none; box-shadow:0 4px 12px rgba(0,0,0,.18);} 
    /* 2) å»é™¤æ•´å¡åŠé€é®ç½©ï¼Œæ”¹ä¸ºåº•éƒ¨æ¸å˜ä¿¡æ¯æ  */
    /* 2) åº•éƒ¨æ¸å˜ä¿¡æ¯æ ï¼šä¸Šç¼“ä¸‹æ€¥ï¼ˆå¤šæ®µè‰²æ ‡æ¨¡æ‹Ÿéçº¿æ€§è¿‡æ¸¡ï¼‰ */
    .info {position:absolute; left:0; right:0; bottom:0; padding:10px; background:linear-gradient(to top,
      rgba(0,0,0,.75) 0%,
      rgba(0,0,0,.60) 35%,
      rgba(0,0,0,.30) 70%,
      rgba(0,0,0,0) 100%
    ); transition: top .25s ease, padding .25s ease;}
    /* æ‚¬åœæ—¶ï¼Œä¿¡æ¯æ æ‰©å±•åˆ°æ•´å¼ å¡ç‰‡ */
    .card:hover .info {top:0;}
    /* å åŠ ä¸€ä¸ªå¯åŠ¨ç”»çš„åŠé€æ˜èƒŒæ™¯å±‚ */
    .info::before {content:""; position:absolute; inset:0; background:rgba(0,0,0,.6); opacity:0; transition:opacity .25s ease;}
    .card:hover .info::before {opacity:1;}
    /* æ–‡æœ¬ç½®äºåŠé€æ˜å±‚ä¹‹ä¸Š */
    .info > * {position:relative; z-index:1;}
    /* 5) æ ‡æ³¨: å¯åœ¨æ­¤è°ƒæ•´æ ‡é¢˜é¢œè‰²ä¸è¡Œè· */
    .info .title {margin:0; font-size:16px; line-height:1.2; color:#ffffff;}
    /* 4) summary æ˜¾ç¤ºä¸¤è¡Œï¼Œå¹¶å¯åœ¨æ­¤è°ƒæ•´é¢œè‰²ä¸è¡Œè· */
    .info .summary {margin:4px 0 0; font-size:12px; line-height:1.4; color:rgba(255,255,255,.9); font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;
      /* è®©å†…å®¹å…ˆè‡ªç„¶æ¢è¡Œåˆ°ç¬¬äºŒè¡Œï¼Œè¶…å‡ºç¬¬äºŒè¡Œå†çœç•¥ */
      white-space: normal; word-break: break-word; overflow: hidden;
      display: -webkit-box; -webkit-box-orient: vertical; -webkit-line-clamp: 2; line-clamp: 2;
    }
    /* hover æ—¶æ˜¾ç¤ºæ›´è¯¦ç»†æè¿°ï¼Œéšè— summary */
    .info .desc {display:none; margin:6px 0 0; font-size:12px; line-height:1.5; color:rgba(255,255,255,.95); font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;} /* å¯è°ƒé¢œè‰²ä¸è¡Œè· */
    .card:hover .info .desc {display:block;}
    .card:hover .info .summary {display:none;}
    /* é¡¶éƒ¨ç±»å‹å¯¼èˆªä¸æŠ˜å æ ·å¼ */
    .topbar {position:sticky; top:0; z-index:10; background: rgba(var(--surface-rgb), .9); padding:8px 0; margin:0 0 12px; box-shadow:0 1px 4px rgba(0,0,0,.06); backdrop-filter: saturate(140%) blur(8px);} 
    .topbar .types {display:flex; gap:8px; flex-wrap:wrap; justify-content:flex-start; padding-left:0;}
    .type-btn {border:1px solid var(--border); background: var(--surface); color: var(--text); padding:6px 12px; border-radius:999px; cursor:pointer; font-size:13px; transition:background .2s, color .2s, border-color .2s, box-shadow .2s;}
    .type-btn:hover {background:#f3f6ff; border-color:#d5def8;}
    .type-btn.active {background: var(--accent); border-color: var(--accent); color:#fff; box-shadow: 0 4px 12px rgba(91,141,239,.3);}    
    .section.collapsed .grid {display:none;}
    .hidden {display:none !important;}

    /* æ ‡é¢˜è¡Œä¸éšè”½æŒ‰é’®æ ·å¼ */
    .title-row {display:flex; align-items:center; gap:8px; padding-top: 10px;}
    .title-row h1 {flex:1 1 auto;}
    .action-right {flex:0 0 auto; display:flex; align-items:center; gap:6px;}
    .search-input {height:30px; padding:0 10px; border:1px solid var(--border); border-radius:16px; font-size:12px; width:160px; background: var(--surface); color: var(--text); transition:border-color .2s, box-shadow .2s;}
    .search-input:focus {outline:none; border-color:#c7d2fe; box-shadow:0 0 0 3px rgba(91,141,239,.18);}    
    .type-btn.ghost {background:transparent; border-color:var(--border); color:var(--muted); padding:6px 10px; font-size:12px; border-radius:999px;}
    .type-btn.ghost:hover {background:#f6f8ff; color:#55617c;}
  </style>
</head>
<body>
  <div class="page">
    <div class="title-row">
      <h1>æˆ‘çš„ç½‘ç«™æ”¶è—</h1>
      <div class="action-right">
        <input id="optional-key" class="search-input" placeholder="è¾“å…¥" />
        <button id="optional-search" class="type-btn ghost" title="æœç´¢">æœç´¢</button>
      </div>
    </div>
    <nav id="topbar" class="topbar"></nav>
    <!-- å†…å®¹å®¹å™¨ -->
    <div id="content"></div>
  </div>

  <!-- å¼•å…¥ç±»å‹æ˜ å°„ -->
  <script src="js/type.js"></script>

  <script>
    /*
      å‡è®¾æ¯ä¸ªæ•°æ®æ–‡ä»¶ä¸­å®šä¹‰äº†å¦‚ä¸‹æ ¼å¼çš„æ•°ç»„ï¼š
      const links = [ { title, url, description } ]
    */
  </script>

  <script>
    const loadScript = src => new Promise((res, rej) => {
      const s = document.createElement('script');
      s.src = src; s.onload = res; s.onerror = () => rej(new Error('åŠ è½½å¤±è´¥:'+src));
      document.head.appendChild(s);
    });

    function createCard(item){
      const a=document.createElement('a'); a.className='card'; a.href=item.url; a.target='_blank'; a.rel='noopener noreferrer';
      if(item.cover) a.style.backgroundImage=`url('${item.cover}')`;
      const info=document.createElement('div'); info.className='info';
      const titleEl=document.createElement('h3'); titleEl.className='title'; titleEl.textContent=item.title;
      const text = item.summary || item.description || '';
      const p=document.createElement('p'); p.className='summary'; p.textContent=text;
      const desc=document.createElement('p'); desc.className='desc'; desc.textContent=item.description || '';
      info.appendChild(titleEl); info.appendChild(p); info.appendChild(desc);
      a.appendChild(info); return a;
    }

    function activateSection(sectionId){
      document.querySelectorAll('.type-btn').forEach(b=>{
        b.classList.toggle('active', b.dataset.target === sectionId);
      });
      document.querySelectorAll('.section').forEach(sec=>{
        sec.classList.toggle('collapsed', sec.id !== sectionId);
      });
      const target = document.getElementById(sectionId);
      if (target) {
        const topbar = document.getElementById('topbar');
        const offset = (topbar ? topbar.offsetHeight : 0) + 8; // é€‚å½“ç•™ç™½
        const y = target.getBoundingClientRect().top + window.pageYOffset - offset;
        window.scrollTo({ top: y, behavior: 'smooth' });
      }
    }

    function render(){
      const content=document.getElementById('content');
      const topbar=document.getElementById('topbar');
      const input = document.getElementById('optional-key');
      const searchBtn = document.getElementById('optional-search');

      // é¡¶éƒ¨æŒ‰é’®
      const btnWrap=document.createElement('div'); btnWrap.className='types';
      btnWrap.setAttribute('role','tablist');

      // å›åˆ°é¡¶éƒ¨æŒ‰é’®
      const homeBtn=document.createElement('button');
      homeBtn.className='type-btn';
      homeBtn.textContent='é¦–é¡µ';
      homeBtn.addEventListener('click',()=>{
        // æ¸…é™¤æ¿€æ´»
        document.querySelectorAll('.type-btn').forEach(b=>b.classList.remove('active'));
        // æŠ˜å æ‰€æœ‰ç±»å‹
        document.querySelectorAll('.section').forEach(sec=>sec.classList.add('collapsed'));
        // å¹³æ»‘æ»šåŠ¨åˆ°æ ‡é¢˜ä½ç½®ï¼ˆè€ƒè™‘é¡¶éƒ¨å¯¼èˆªé«˜åº¦åç§»ï¼‰
        const topbar = document.getElementById('topbar');
        const header = document.querySelector('.title-row') || document.querySelector('h1');
        const offset = (topbar ? topbar.offsetHeight : 0) + 8;
        const y = (header ? header.getBoundingClientRect().top + window.pageYOffset : 0) - offset;
        window.scrollTo({ top: y, behavior: 'smooth' });
      });
      btnWrap.appendChild(homeBtn);

      types.forEach((t, idx)=>{
        const store=window.linkStore||{}; const data=store[t.id];
        if(!Array.isArray(data) || !data.length) return;

        // section
        const section=document.createElement('section');
        section.className='section';
        section.id = `section-${t.id}`;
        section.dataset.optional = t.optional ? '1' : '0';
        section.innerHTML=`<h2 class=\"type-title\" data-target=\"section-${t.id}\">${t.name}</h2>`;
        const grid=document.createElement('div'); grid.className='grid';
        data.forEach(item=>grid.appendChild(createCard(item)));
        section.appendChild(grid);
        content.appendChild(section);

        // nav button
        const btn=document.createElement('button');
        btn.className='type-btn';
        btn.textContent=t.name;
        btn.dataset.target = section.id;
        btn.dataset.optional = t.optional ? '1' : '0';
        btn.setAttribute('role','tab');
        btn.addEventListener('click',()=>{
          activateSection(section.id);
        });
        btnWrap.appendChild(btn);
      });

      topbar.appendChild(btnWrap);

      // åˆ‡æ¢å¯é€‰ç±»å‹æ˜¾ç¤º/éšè—
      let optionalShown = false;
      const syncOptionalVisibility = () => {
        document.querySelectorAll('[data-optional=\'1\']').forEach(el=>{
          el.classList.toggle('hidden', !optionalShown);
        });
      };
      function handleSearch(){
        const v = (input.value || '').trim();
        if (v === '72875') { optionalShown = true; syncOptionalVisibility(); }
        else if (v === '0') { optionalShown = false; syncOptionalVisibility(); }
      }
      searchBtn.addEventListener('click', handleSearch);
      input.addEventListener('keydown', (e)=>{ if (e.key === 'Enter') handleSearch(); });
      // åˆå§‹åŒ–ä¸€æ¬¡
      syncOptionalVisibility();

      // å†…å®¹æ ‡é¢˜ç‚¹å‡»åŒæ ·å¯æŠ˜å /å±•å¼€å¹¶å®šä½
      content.addEventListener('click', (e)=>{
        const h = e.target.closest('.type-title');
        if (!h) return;
        const targetId = h.dataset.target;
        if (targetId) activateSection(targetId);
      });

      // é»˜è®¤ä¸æ»šåŠ¨åˆ°ä»»ä½•ç±»å‹ï¼Œä¿æŒåœ¨é¡¶éƒ¨
      document.querySelectorAll('.section').forEach(sec=>sec.classList.add('collapsed'));
    }

    Promise.all(types.map(t=>loadScript(t.file))).then(render).catch(console.error);
  </script>
</body>
</html>

```

- æ¨ªå‘æ»šåŠ¨æ¡ä¸è£å‰ªçš„åŸå› ï¼š`.page` ä½¿ç”¨ç™¾åˆ†æ¯”å·¦å³å†…è¾¹è·æ—¶ï¼Œè‹¥æœªè®¾ box-sizingï¼Œä¼šæŒ‰å†…å®¹ç›’è®¡ç®—ï¼Œå¯¼è‡´æ€»å®½åº¦è¶…è¿‡ 100%ã€‚æˆ‘å·²ä¸ºå…¨å±€åŠ äº† `box-sizing: border-box;` å¹¶ä¿è¯ `.page` ä¹Ÿæ˜¯ border-boxï¼Œä»è€Œæ¶ˆé™¤æ¨ªå‘æº¢å‡ºä¸è£å‰ªï¼Œå†…å®¹ä¸€å±æ˜¾ç¤ºæ— éœ€æ¨ªå‘æ»šåŠ¨ã€‚
- å­—ä½“è°ƒæ•´ï¼šå°†å¡ç‰‡çš„ `summary` ä¸è¯¦ç»†æè¿° `desc` æŒ‡å®šä¸ºç³»ç»Ÿé»˜è®¤å­—ä½“æ— `Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif`ï¼Œä¸å—å…¨å±€è‡ªå®šä¹‰å­—ä½“å½±å“ã€‚

---

**User**

1. å°†ç±»å‹å¯¼èˆªéƒ¨åˆ†ä¸­çš„é¦–é¡µæŒ‰é’®è·ç¦»å·¦è¾¹çš„è·ç¦»å’Œç±»å‹å¯¼èˆªå†…æŒ‰é’®é—´è·ä¿æŒä¸€è‡´ï¼Œ 2 å°†æ–°å¢çš„å­—ä½“è·¯å¾„æ”¹ä¸ºres/fontç›®å½•ä¸‹

---

**Cursor**

I'll update the nav spacing to use a single CSS variable for both the left padding and inter-button gap, making the é¦–é¡µ button offset match the internal spacing. I'll also change the font source path to res/font/SmileySans-Oblique.ttf. Proceeding to edit index.html.

```html
      const links = [ { title, url, description } ]
    */
  </script>

  <script>
    const loadScript = src => new Promise((res, rej) => {
      const s = document.createElement('script');
      s.src = src; s.onload = res; s.onerror = () => rej(new Error('åŠ è½½å¤±è´¥:'+src));
      document.head.appendChild(s);
    });

    function createCard(item){
      const a=document.createElement('a'); a.className='card'; a.href=item.url; a.target='_blank'; a.rel='noopener noreferrer';
      if(item.cover) a.style.backgroundImage=`url('${item.cover}')`;
      const info=document.createElement('div'); info.className='info';
      const titleEl=document.createElement('h3'); titleEl.className='title'; titleEl.textContent=item.title;
      const text = item.summary || item.description || '';
      const p=document.createElement('p'); p.className='summary'; p.textContent=text;
      const desc=document.createElement('p'); desc.className='desc'; desc.textContent=item.description || '';
      info.appendChild(titleEl); info.appendChild(p); info.appendChild(desc);
      a.appendChild(info); return a;
    }

    function activateSection(sectionId){
      document.querySelectorAll('.type-btn').forEach(b=>{
        b.classList.toggle('active', b.dataset.target === sectionId);
      });
      document.querySelectorAll('.section').forEach(sec=>{
        sec.classList.toggle('collapsed', sec.id !== sectionId);
      });
      const target = document.getElementById(sectionId);
      if (target) {
        const topbar = document.getElementById('topbar');
        const offset = (topbar ? topbar.offsetHeight : 0) + 8; // é€‚å½“ç•™ç™½
        const y = target.getBoundingClientRect().top + window.pageYOffset - offset;
        window.scrollTo({ top: y, behavior: 'smooth' });
      }
    }

    function render(){
      const content=document.getElementById('content');
      const topbar=document.getElementById('topbar');
      const input = document.getElementById('optional-key');
      const searchBtn = document.getElementById('optional-search');

      // é¡¶éƒ¨æŒ‰é’®
      const btnWrap=document.createElement('div'); btnWrap.className='types';
      btnWrap.setAttribute('role','tablist');

      // å›åˆ°é¡¶éƒ¨æŒ‰é’®
      const homeBtn=document.createElement('button');
      homeBtn.className='type-btn';
      homeBtn.textContent='é¦–é¡µ';
      homeBtn.addEventListener('click',()=>{
        // æ¸…é™¤æ¿€æ´»
        document.querySelectorAll('.type-btn').forEach(b=>b.classList.remove('active'));
        // æŠ˜å æ‰€æœ‰ç±»å‹
        document.querySelectorAll('.section').forEach(sec=>sec.classList.add('collapsed'));
        // å¹³æ»‘æ»šåŠ¨åˆ°æ ‡é¢˜ä½ç½®ï¼ˆè€ƒè™‘é¡¶éƒ¨å¯¼èˆªé«˜åº¦åç§»ï¼‰
        const topbar = document.getElementById('topbar');
        const header = document.querySelector('.title-row') || document.querySelector('h1');
        const offset = (topbar ? topbar.offsetHeight : 0) + 8;
        const y = (header ? header.getBoundingClientRect().top + window.pageYOffset : 0) - offset;
        window.scrollTo({ top: y, behavior: 'smooth' });
      });
      btnWrap.appendChild(homeBtn);

      types.forEach((t, idx)=>{
        const store=window.linkStore||{}; const data=store[t.id];
        if(!Array.isArray(data) || !data.length) return;

        // section
        const section=document.createElement('section');
        section.className='section';
        section.id = `section-${t.id}`;
        section.dataset.optional = t.optional ? '1' : '0';
        section.innerHTML=`<h2 class=\"type-title\" data-target=\"section-${t.id}\">${t.name}</h2>`;
        const grid=document.createElement('div'); grid.className='grid';
        data.forEach(item=>grid.appendChild(createCard(item)));
        section.appendChild(grid);
        content.appendChild(section);

        // nav button
        const btn=document.createElement('button');
        btn.className='type-btn';
        btn.textContent=t.name;
        btn.dataset.target = section.id;
        btn.dataset.optional = t.optional ? '1' : '0';
        btn.setAttribute('role','tab');
        btn.addEventListener('click',()=>{
          activateSection(section.id);
        });
        btnWrap.appendChild(btn);
      });

      topbar.appendChild(btnWrap);

      // åˆ‡æ¢å¯é€‰ç±»å‹æ˜¾ç¤º/éšè—
      let optionalShown = false;
      const syncOptionalVisibility = () => {
        document.querySelectorAll('[data-optional=\'1\']').forEach(el=>{
          el.classList.toggle('hidden', !optionalShown);
        });
      };
      function handleSearch(){
        const v = (input.value || '').trim();
        if (v === '72875') { optionalShown = true; syncOptionalVisibility(); }
        else if (v === '0') { optionalShown = false; syncOptionalVisibility(); }
      }
      searchBtn.addEventListener('click', handleSearch);
      input.addEventListener('keydown', (e)=>{ if (e.key === 'Enter') handleSearch(); });
      // åˆå§‹åŒ–ä¸€æ¬¡
      syncOptionalVisibility();

      // å†…å®¹æ ‡é¢˜ç‚¹å‡»åŒæ ·å¯æŠ˜å /å±•å¼€å¹¶å®šä½
      content.addEventListener('click', (e)=>{
        const h = e.target.closest('.type-title');
        if (!h) return;
        const targetId = h.dataset.target;
        if (targetId) activateSection(targetId);
      });

      // é»˜è®¤ä¸æ»šåŠ¨åˆ°ä»»ä½•ç±»å‹ï¼Œä¿æŒåœ¨é¡¶éƒ¨
      document.querySelectorAll('.section').forEach(sec=>sec.classList.add('collapsed'));
    }

    Promise.all(types.map(t=>loadScript(t.file))).then(render).catch(console.error);
  </script>
</body>
</html>

```

- é¦–é¡µæŒ‰é’®å·¦ä¾§é—´è·å·²ä¸ç±»å‹æŒ‰é’®é—´è·ç»Ÿä¸€ï¼šé€šè¿‡ `--nav-gap` æ§åˆ¶ï¼Œ`.topbar .types` ä½¿ç”¨ `gap: var(--nav-gap)` ä¸” `padding-left: var(--nav-gap)`ã€‚
- å­—ä½“è·¯å¾„å·²æ”¹ä¸º `res/font/SmileySans-Oblique.ttf`ã€‚
